# <a name="routing-in-aspnet-core"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-103">Routing in ASP.NET Core</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-103">Routing in ASP.NET Core</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-104">Di [Ryan Nowak](https://github.com/rynowak), [Kirk Larkin](https://twitter.com/serpent5)e [Rick Anderson](https://twitter.com/RickAndMSFT)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-104">By [Ryan Nowak](https://github.com/rynowak), [Kirk Larkin](https://twitter.com/serpent5), and [Rick Anderson](https://twitter.com/RickAndMSFT)</span></span>

::: moniker range=">= aspnetcore-3.0"

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-105">Il routing è responsabile della corrispondenza delle richieste HTTP in ingresso e dell'invio di tali richieste agli endpoint eseguibili dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-105">Routing is responsible for matching incoming HTTP requests and dispatching those requests to the app's executable endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-106">Gli [endpoint](#endpoint) sono le unità dell'app del codice di gestione delle richieste eseguibile.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-106">[Endpoints](#endpoint) are the app's units of executable request-handling code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-107">Gli endpoint vengono definiti nell'app e configurati all'avvio dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-107">Endpoints are defined in the app and configured when the app starts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-108">Il processo di corrispondenza dell'endpoint può estrarre valori dall'URL della richiesta e fornire tali valori per l'elaborazione della richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-108">The endpoint matching process can extract values from the request's URL and provide those values for request processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-109">Usando le informazioni sull'endpoint dall'app, il routing è anche in grado di generare URL con mapping agli endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-109">Using endpoint information from the app, routing is also able to generate URLs that map to endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-110">Le app possono configurare il routing tramite:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-110">Apps can configure routing using:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="3658d-111">Controller</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-111">Controllers</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="3658d-112">Razor Pages</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-112">Razor Pages</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="3658d-113">SignalR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-113">SignalR</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="3658d-114">Servizi gRPC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-114">gRPC Services</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="3658d-115">[Middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) abilitato per gli endpoint, ad esempio i [controlli di integrità](xref:host-and-deploy/health-checks).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-115">Endpoint-enabled [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) such as [Health Checks](xref:host-and-deploy/health-checks).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="3658d-116">Delegati e espressioni lambda registrate con il routing.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-116">Delegates and lambdas registered with routing.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-117">In questo documento vengono illustrati i dettagli di basso livello del routing ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-117">This document covers low-level details of ASP.NET Core routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-118">Per informazioni sulla configurazione del routing:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-118">For information on configuring routing:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-119">Per i controller, vedere <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-119">For controllers, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-120">Per Razor Pages convenzioni, vedere <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-120">For Razor Pages conventions, see <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-121">Il sistema di routing degli endpoint descritto in questo documento si applica a ASP.NET Core 3,0 e versioni successive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-121">The endpoint routing system described in this document applies to ASP.NET Core 3.0 and later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-122">Per informazioni sul sistema di routing precedente basato su <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>, selezionare la versione ASP.NET Core 2,1 usando uno degli approcci seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-122">For information on the previous routing system based on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>, select the ASP.NET Core 2.1 version using one of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-123">Selettore di versione per una versione precedente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-123">The version selector for a previous version.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-124">Selezionare [ASP.NET Core 2,1 routing](https://docs.microsoft.com/aspnet/core/fundamentals/routing?view=aspnetcore-2.1).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-124">Select [ASP.NET Core 2.1 routing](https://docs.microsoft.com/aspnet/core/fundamentals/routing?view=aspnetcore-2.1).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-125">[Visualizzare o scaricare il codice di esempio](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples/3.x) ([procedura per il download](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-125">[View or download sample code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples/3.x) ([how to download](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-126">Gli esempi di download per questo documento sono abilitati da una classe di `Startup` specifica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-126">The download samples for this document are enabled by a specific `Startup` class.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-127">Per eseguire un esempio specifico, modificare *Program.cs* per chiamare la classe `Startup` desiderata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-127">To run a specific sample, modify *Program.cs* to call the desired `Startup` class.</span></span>

## <a name="routing-basics"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-128">Nozioni fondamentali sul routing</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-128">Routing basics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-129">Tutti i modelli di ASP.NET Core includono il routing nel codice generato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-129">All ASP.NET Core templates include routing in the generated code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-130">Il routing viene registrato nella pipeline [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) in `Startup.Configure`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-130">Routing is registered in the [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) pipeline in `Startup.Configure`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-131">Il codice seguente illustra un esempio di routing di base:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-131">The following code shows a basic example of routing:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet&highlight=8,10)]

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-132">Il routing usa una coppia di middleware, registrato da <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*> e <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-132">Routing uses a pair of middleware, registered by <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-133">`UseRouting` aggiunge la corrispondenza della route alla pipeline middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-133">`UseRouting` adds route matching to the middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-134">Questo middleware esamina il set di endpoint definiti nell'app e seleziona la [migliore corrispondenza](#urlm) in base alla richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-134">This middleware looks at the set of endpoints defined in the app, and selects the [best match](#urlm) based on the request.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-135">`UseEndpoints` aggiunge l'esecuzione dell'endpoint alla pipeline middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-135">`UseEndpoints` adds endpoint execution to the middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-136">Esegue il delegato associato all'endpoint selezionato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-136">It runs the delegate associated with the selected endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-137">L'esempio precedente include una singola *Route per l'endpoint di codice* usando il metodo [MapGet](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*) :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-137">The preceding example includes a single *route to code* endpoint using the [MapGet](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*) method:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-138">Quando una richiesta HTTP `GET` viene inviata all'URL radice `/`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-138">When an HTTP `GET` request is sent to the root URL `/`:</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-139">Il delegato della richiesta visualizzato viene eseguito.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-139">The request delegate shown executes.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-140">`Hello World!` viene scritto nella risposta HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-140">`Hello World!` is written to the HTTP response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-141">Per impostazione predefinita, l'URL radice `/` è `https://localhost:5001/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-141">By default, the root URL `/` is `https://localhost:5001/`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-142">Se il metodo di richiesta non è `GET` o l'URL radice non è `/`, non viene restituita alcuna corrispondenza e viene restituito un HTTP 404.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-142">If the request method is not `GET` or the root URL is not `/`, no route matches and an HTTP 404 is returned.</span></span>

### <a name="endpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-143">Endpoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-143">Endpoint</span></span>

<a name="endpoint"></a>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-144">Il metodo `MapGet` viene utilizzato per definire un **endpoint**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-144">The `MapGet` method is used to define an **endpoint**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-145">Un endpoint è un elemento che può essere:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-145">An endpoint is something that can be:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-146">Selezionato, associando l'URL e il metodo HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-146">Selected, by matching the URL and HTTP method.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-147">Eseguita eseguendo il delegato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-147">Executed, by running the delegate.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-148">Gli endpoint che possono essere confrontati ed eseguiti dall'app sono configurati in `UseEndpoints`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-148">Endpoints that can be matched and executed by the app are configured in `UseEndpoints`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-149">Ad esempio, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>e [metodi simili](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions) connettono i delegati della richiesta al sistema di routing.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-149">For example, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>, and [similar methods](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions) connect request delegates to the routing system.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="3658d-150">Per connettere ASP.NET Core funzionalità del Framework al sistema di routing, è possibile utilizzare metodi aggiuntivi:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-150">Additional methods can be used to connect ASP.NET Core framework features to the routing system:</span></span>
- [<span data-ttu-id="3658d-151">MapRazorPages per Razor Pages</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-151">MapRazorPages for Razor Pages</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RazorPagesEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRazorPages*)
- [<span data-ttu-id="3658d-152">MapControllers per i controller</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-152">MapControllers for controllers</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllers*)
- [<span data-ttu-id="3658d-153">> MapHub\<THub per SignalR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-153">MapHub\<THub> for SignalR</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.SignalR.HubRouteBuilder.MapHub*) 
- [<span data-ttu-id="3658d-154">MapGrpcService\<TService > per gRPC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-154">MapGrpcService\<TService> for gRPC</span></span>](xref:grpc/aspnetcore)

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-155">Nell'esempio seguente viene illustrato il routing con un modello di route più sofisticato:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-155">The following example shows routing with a more sophisticated route template:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-156">La stringa `/hello/{name:alpha}` è un **modello di route**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-156">The string `/hello/{name:alpha}` is a **route template**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-157">Viene usato per configurare la corrispondenza con l'endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-157">It is used to configure how the endpoint is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-158">In questo caso, il modello corrisponde a:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-158">In this case, the template matches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-159">Un URL come `/hello/Ryan`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-159">A URL like `/hello/Ryan`</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-160">Qualsiasi percorso URL che inizia con `/hello/` seguito da una sequenza di caratteri alfabetici.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-160">Any URL path that begins with `/hello/` followed by a sequence of alphabetic characters.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="3658d-161">`:alpha` applica un vincolo di route che corrisponde solo ai caratteri alfabetici.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-161">`:alpha` applies a route constraint that matches only alphabetic characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-162">I [vincoli di route](#route-constraint-reference) vengono illustrati più avanti in questo documento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-162">[Route constraints](#route-constraint-reference) are explained later in this document.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-163">Il secondo segmento del percorso URL, `{name:alpha}`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-163">The second segment of the URL path, `{name:alpha}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-164">Viene associato al parametro `name`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-164">Is bound to the `name` parameter.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-165">Viene acquisito e archiviato in [HttpRequest. routeValues](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.RouteValues*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-165">Is captured and stored in [HttpRequest.RouteValues](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.RouteValues*).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-166">Il sistema di routing degli endpoint descritto in questo documento è nuovo a partire da ASP.NET Core 3,0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-166">The endpoint routing system described in this document is new as of ASP.NET Core 3.0.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-167">Tuttavia, tutte le versioni di ASP.NET Core supportano lo stesso set di funzionalità del modello di route e vincoli di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-167">However, all versions of ASP.NET Core support the same set of route template features and route constraints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-169">Nell'esempio precedente viene illustrato come:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-169">The preceding example demonstrates how:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-170">Il middleware di autorizzazione può essere usato con il routing.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-170">The authorization middleware can be used with routing.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-171">Gli endpoint possono essere usati per configurare il comportamento di autorizzazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-171">Endpoints can be used to configure authorization behavior.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-172">La chiamata di <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapHealthChecks*> aggiunge un endpoint di controllo integrità.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-172">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapHealthChecks*> call adds a health check endpoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-173">Il concatenamento di <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthorizationEndpointConventionBuilderExtensions.RequireAuthorization*> a questa chiamata collega un criterio di autorizzazione all'endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-173">Chaining <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthorizationEndpointConventionBuilderExtensions.RequireAuthorization*> on to this call attaches an authorization policy to the endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-174">La chiamata di <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthAppBuilderExtensions.UseAuthentication*> e <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthorizationAppBuilderExtensions.UseAuthorization*> aggiunge il middleware di autenticazione e autorizzazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-174">Calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthAppBuilderExtensions.UseAuthentication*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthorizationAppBuilderExtensions.UseAuthorization*> adds the authentication and authorization middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-175">Questi middleware vengono inseriti tra <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*> e `UseEndpoints` in modo che possano:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-175">These middleware are placed between <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*> and `UseEndpoints` so that they can:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-176">Vedere quale endpoint è stato selezionato da `UseRouting`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-176">See which endpoint was selected by `UseRouting`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-177">Applicare un criterio di autorizzazione prima che <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> invii all'endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-177">Apply an authorization policy before <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> dispatches to the endpoint.</span></span>

<a name="metadata"></a>

### <a name="endpoint-metadata"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-178">Metadati dell'endpoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-178">Endpoint metadata</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-179">Nell'esempio precedente sono presenti due endpoint, ma solo l'endpoint di controllo integrità dispone di un criterio di autorizzazione collegato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-179">In the preceding example, there are two endpoints, but only the health check endpoint has an authorization policy attached.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-180">Se la richiesta corrisponde all'endpoint di controllo integrità, `/healthz`viene eseguito un controllo di autorizzazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-180">If the request matches the health check endpoint, `/healthz`, an authorization check is performed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-181">Ciò dimostra che gli endpoint possono avere dati aggiuntivi collegati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-181">This demonstrates that endpoints can have extra data attached to them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-182">Questi dati aggiuntivi sono detti **metadati**dell'endpoint:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-182">This extra data is called endpoint **metadata**:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-183">I metadati possono essere elaborati dal middleware compatibile con il routing.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-183">The metadata can be processed by routing-aware middleware.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-184">I metadati possono essere di qualsiasi tipo .NET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-184">The metadata can be of any .NET type.</span></span>

## <a name="routing-concepts"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-185">Concetti di routing</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-185">Routing concepts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-186">Il sistema di routing si basa sulla pipeline middleware aggiungendo il concetto di **endpoint** potente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-186">The routing system builds on top of the middleware pipeline by adding the powerful **endpoint** concept.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-187">Gli endpoint rappresentano unità della funzionalità dell'app che sono diverse l'una dall'altra in termini di routing, autorizzazione e numero di sistemi ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-187">Endpoints represent units of the app's functionality that are distinct from each other in terms of routing, authorization, and any number of ASP.NET Core's systems.</span></span>

<a name="endpoint"></a>

### <a name="aspnet-core-endpoint-definition"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-188">Definizione di endpoint ASP.NET Core</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-188">ASP.NET Core endpoint definition</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-189">Un endpoint ASP.NET Core è:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-189">An ASP.NET Core endpoint is:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-190">Eseguibile: ha un <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-190">Executable: Has a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-191">Extensible: include una raccolta di [metadati](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.Metadata*) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-191">Extensible: Has a [Metadata](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.Metadata*) collection.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-192">Selectable: dispone facoltativamente [delle informazioni di routing](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.RoutePattern*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-192">Selectable: Optionally, has [routing information](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.RoutePattern*).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-193">Enumerable: la raccolta di endpoint può essere elencata recuperando il <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointDataSource> da [di](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-193">Enumerable: The collection of endpoints can be listed by retrieving the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointDataSource> from [DI](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-194">Il codice seguente illustra come recuperare e controllare l'endpoint che corrisponde alla richiesta corrente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-194">The following code shows how to retrieve and inspect the endpoint matching the current request:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-211">Il middleware dopo `UseEndpoints` viene eseguito solo quando non viene trovata alcuna corrispondenza.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-211">The middleware after `UseEndpoints` execute only when no match is found.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-212">Il middleware `UseRouting` usa il metodo [seendpoint](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.SetEndpoint*) per aggiungere l'endpoint al contesto corrente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-212">The `UseRouting` middleware uses the [SetEndpoint](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.SetEndpoint*) method to attach the endpoint to the current context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-213">È possibile sostituire il middleware `UseRouting` con la logica personalizzata e ottenere comunque i vantaggi derivanti dall'uso degli endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-213">It's possible to replace the `UseRouting` middleware with custom logic and still get the benefits of using endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-214">Gli endpoint sono una primitiva di basso livello, ad esempio middleware, e non sono associati all'implementazione del routing.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-214">Endpoints are a low-level primitive like middleware, and aren't coupled to the routing implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-215">Per la maggior parte delle app non è necessario sostituire `UseRouting` con la logica personalizzata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-215">Most apps don't need to replace `UseRouting` with custom logic.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-216">Il middleware `UseEndpoints` è progettato per essere usato in combinazione con il middleware di `UseRouting`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-216">The `UseEndpoints` middleware is designed to be used in tandem with the `UseRouting` middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-217">La logica di base per l'esecuzione di un endpoint non è complessa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-217">The core logic to execute an endpoint isn't complicated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-218">Utilizzare <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.GetEndpoint*> per recuperare l'endpoint e quindi richiamare la relativa proprietà <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-218">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.GetEndpoint*> to retrieve the endpoint, and then invoke its <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate> property.</span></span>

    * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-222">In genere il middleware visualizzato prima che il routing modifichi una proprietà della richiesta, ad esempio <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RewriteBuilderExtensions.UseRewriter*>, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HttpMethodOverrideExtensions.UseHttpMethodOverride*>o <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.UsePathBaseExtensions.UsePathBase*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-222">Usually middleware that appears before routing modifies some property of the request, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RewriteBuilderExtensions.UseRewriter*>, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HttpMethodOverrideExtensions.UseHttpMethodOverride*>, or <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.UsePathBaseExtensions.UsePathBase*>.</span></span>

    * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-224">Middleware che esegue tra `UseRouting` e `UseEndpoints`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-224">Middleware that runs between `UseRouting` and `UseEndpoints`:</span></span>
      * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-225">In genere controlla i metadati per comprendere gli endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-225">Usually inspects metadata to understand the endpoints.</span></span>
      * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-226">Consente spesso di prendere decisioni di sicurezza, come avviene per `UseAuthorization` e `UseCors`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-226">Often makes security decisions, as done by `UseAuthorization` and `UseCors`.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-227">La combinazione di middleware e metadati consente la configurazione dei criteri per endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-227">The combination of middleware and metadata allows configuring policies per-endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-228">Il codice precedente mostra un esempio di middleware personalizzato che supporta i criteri per endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-228">The preceding code shows an example of a custom middleware that supports per-endpoint policies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-229">Il middleware scrive un *log di controllo* di accesso ai dati sensibili nella console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-229">The middleware writes an *audit log* of access to sensitive data to the console.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-230">Il middleware può essere configurato per *controllare* un endpoint con i metadati del `AuditPolicyAttribute`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-230">The middleware can be configured to *audit* an endpoint with the `AuditPolicyAttribute` metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-231">In questo esempio viene illustrato un modello *di consenso only endpoints that are marked as sensitive are audited.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-232">È possibile definire questa logica in senso inverso, ad esempio controllando tutti gli elementi che non sono contrassegnati come sicuri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-232">It's possible to define this logic in reverse, auditing everything that isn't marked as safe, for flexible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-234">Questa logica può essere progettata nel modo più adatto al caso d'uso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-234">This logic could be designed in whatever way suits the use case.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-240">I metadati dei criteri di controllo `AuditPolicyAttribute` sono definiti come `Attribute` per un uso più semplice con Framework basati su classi quali controller e SignalR.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-240">The audit policy metadata `AuditPolicyAttribute` is defined as an `Attribute` for easier use with class-based frameworks such as controllers and SignalR.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-241">Quando si usa la *Route per il codice*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-241">When using *route to code*:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-242">I metadati sono collegati a un'API del generatore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-242">Metadata is attached with a builder API.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-243">I Framework basati su classi includono tutti gli attributi nel metodo e nella classe corrispondenti durante la creazione degli endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-243">Class-based frameworks include all attributes on the corresponding method and class when creating endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-244">Le procedure consigliate per i tipi di metadati sono definirle come interfacce o attributi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-244">The best practices for metadata types are to define them either as interfaces or attributes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-245">Interfacce e attributi consentono il riutilizzo del codice.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-245">Interfaces and attributes allow code reuse.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-246">Il sistema dei metadati è flessibile e non impone alcuna restrizione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-246">The metadata system is flexible and doesn't impose any limitations.</span></span>

<a name="tm"></a>

### <a name="comparing-a-terminal-middleware-and-routing"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-247">Confronto tra un middleware terminale e il routing</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-247">Comparing a terminal middleware and routing</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-248">L'esempio di codice seguente contrasta l'uso del middleware con l'uso del routing:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-248">The following code sample contrasts using middleware with using routing:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/TerminalMiddlewareStartup.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-249">Lo stile del middleware visualizzato con `Approach 1:` è **middleware terminale**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-249">The style of middleware shown with `Approach 1:` is **terminal middleware**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-250">Viene chiamato middleware terminale perché esegue un'operazione di corrispondenza:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-250">It's called terminal middleware because it does a matching operation:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-251">L'operazione di corrispondenza nell'esempio precedente è `Path == "/"` per il middleware e `Path == "/Movie"` per il routing.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-251">The matching operation in the preceding sample is `Path == "/"` for the middleware and `Path == "/Movie"` for routing.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-252">Quando una corrispondenza ha esito positivo, vengono eseguite alcune funzionalità e viene restituito, anziché richiamare il middleware `next`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-252">When a match is successful, it executes some functionality and returns, rather than invoking the `next` middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-253">Viene chiamato middleware del middleware terminale perché termina la ricerca, esegue alcune funzionalità e quindi restituisce.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-253">It's called terminal middleware middleware because it terminates the search, executes some functionality, and then returns.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-254">Confronto tra un middleware terminale e il routing:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-254">Comparing a terminal middleware and routing:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-255">Entrambi gli approcci consentono di terminare la pipeline di elaborazione:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-255">Both approaches allow terminating the processing pipeline:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-256">Il middleware termina la pipeline restituendo anziché richiamare `next`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-256">Middleware terminates the pipeline by returning rather than invoking `next`.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-257">Gli endpoint sono sempre terminali.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-257">Endpoints are always terminal.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-258">Il middleware terminale consente di posizionare il middleware in una posizione arbitraria nella pipeline:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-258">Terminal middleware allows positioning the middleware at an arbitrary place in the pipeline:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-259">Gli endpoint vengono eseguiti in corrispondenza della posizione del <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-259">Endpoints execute at the position of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-260">Il middleware terminale consente il codice arbitrario per determinare quando il middleware corrisponde a:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-260">Terminal middleware allows arbitrary code to determine when the middleware matches:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-261">Il codice personalizzato per la corrispondenza delle route può essere dettagliato e difficile da scrivere correttamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-261">Custom route matching code can be verbose and difficult to write correctly.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-262">Il routing fornisce soluzioni semplici per le app tipiche.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-262">Routing provides straightforward solutions for typical apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-263">La maggior parte delle app non richiede codice personalizzato per la corrispondenza delle route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-263">Most apps don't require custom route matching code.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-264">L'interfaccia degli endpoint con middleware, ad esempio `UseAuthorization` e `UseCors`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-264">Endpoints interface with middleware such as `UseAuthorization` and `UseCors`.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-265">L'uso di un middleware terminale con `UseAuthorization` o `UseCors` richiede l'interazione manuale con il sistema di autorizzazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-265">Using a terminal middleware with `UseAuthorization` or `UseCors` requires manual interfacing with the authorization system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-266">Un [endpoint](#endpoint) definisce entrambi:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-266">An [endpoint](#endpoint) defines both:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-267">Delegato per l'elaborazione delle richieste.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-267">A delegate to process requests.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-268">Raccolta di metadati arbitrari.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-268">A collection of arbitrary metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-269">I metadati vengono usati per implementare le problematiche trasversali in base ai criteri e alla configurazione collegati a ogni endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-269">The metadata is used to implement cross-cutting concerns based on policies and configuration attached to each endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-270">Il middleware terminale può essere uno strumento efficace, ma può richiedere:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-270">Terminal middleware can be an effective tool, but can require:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-271">Una quantità significativa di codice e test.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-271">A significant amount of coding and testing.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-272">Integrazione manuale con altri sistemi per raggiungere il livello di flessibilità desiderato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-272">Manual integration with other systems to achieve the desired level of flexibility.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-273">Prendere in considerazione l'integrazione con routing prima di scrivere un middleware terminale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-273">Consider integrating with routing before writing a terminal middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-274">Il middleware terminale esistente che si integra con [Map](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index#branch-the-middleware-pipeline) o <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapWhenExtensions.MapWhen*> in genere può essere trasformato in un endpoint in grado di riconoscere il routing.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-274">Existing terminal middleware that integrates with [Map](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index#branch-the-middleware-pipeline) or <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapWhenExtensions.MapWhen*> can usually be turned into a routing aware endpoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-275">[MapHealthChecks](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/Middleware/HealthChecks/src/Builder/HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.cs#L16) illustra il modello per il router-Ware:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-275">[MapHealthChecks](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/Middleware/HealthChecks/src/Builder/HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.cs#L16) demonstrates the pattern for router-ware:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-276">Scrivere un metodo di estensione su <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-276">Write an extension method on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder>.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-278">Alleghi il middleware alla nuova pipeline.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-278">Attach the middleware to the new pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-279">In questo caso, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseHealthChecks*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-279">In this case, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseHealthChecks*>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-280"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IApplicationBuilder.Build*> la pipeline middleware in una <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-280"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IApplicationBuilder.Build*> the middleware pipeline into a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-281">Chiamare `Map` e fornire la nuova pipeline middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-281">Call `Map` and provide the new middleware pipeline.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-282">Restituisce l'oggetto generatore fornito da `Map` dal metodo di estensione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-282">Return the builder object provided by `Map` from the extension method.</span></span>

<a name="urlm"></a>

### <a name="url-matching"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-289">Corrispondenza URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-289">URL matching</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-290">È il processo mediante il quale il routing corrisponde a una richiesta in ingresso a un [endpoint](#endpoint).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-290">Is the process by which routing matches an incoming request to an [endpoint](#endpoint).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-291">Si basa sui dati nel percorso e nelle intestazioni URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-291">Is based on data in the URL path and headers.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-292">Può essere esteso per considerare tutti i dati nella richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-292">Can be extended to consider any data in the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-293">Quando viene eseguito un middleware di routing, imposta un `Endpoint` e indirizza i valori a una [funzionalità di richiesta](xref:fundamentals/request-features) sul <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpContext> dalla richiesta corrente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-293">When a routing middleware executes, it sets an `Endpoint` and route values to a [request feature](xref:fundamentals/request-features) on the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpContext> from the current request:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-294">La chiamata a [HttpContext. GetEndPoint](<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.GetEndpoint*>) Ottiene l'endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-294">Calling [HttpContext.GetEndpoint](<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.GetEndpoint*>) gets the endpoint.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-295">`HttpRequest.RouteValues` ottiene la raccolta dei valori di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-295">`HttpRequest.RouteValues` gets the collection of route values.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-296">Il [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) eseguito dopo il middleware di routing può ispezionare l'endpoint ed eseguire un'azione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-296">[Middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) running after the routing middleware can inspect the endpoint and take action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-297">Un middleware di autorizzazione, ad esempio, può interrogare la raccolta di metadati dell'endpoint per i criteri di autorizzazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-297">For example, an authorization middleware can interrogate the endpoint's metadata collection for an authorization policy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-298">Dopo l'esecuzione di tutto il middleware nella pipeline di elaborazione della richiesta, viene richiamato il delegato dell'endpoint selezionato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-298">After all of the middleware in the request processing pipeline is executed, the selected endpoint's delegate is invoked.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-299">Il sistema di routing nell'endpoint di routing è responsabile di tutte le decisioni relative all'invio.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-299">The routing system in endpoint routing is responsible for all dispatching decisions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-300">Poiché il middleware applica criteri basati sull'endpoint selezionato, è importante:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-300">Because the middleware applies policies based on the selected endpoint, it's important that:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-301">Qualsiasi decisione che può influire sull'invio o sull'applicazione di criteri di sicurezza viene effettuata all'interno del sistema di routing.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-301">Any decision that can affect dispatching or the application of security policies is made inside the routing system.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-302">Per la compatibilità con le versioni precedenti, quando viene eseguito un controller o un Razor Pages delegato dell'endpoint, le proprietà di [RouteContext. RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) vengono impostate sui valori appropriati in base all'elaborazione della richiesta eseguita fino a questo punto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-302">For backwards-compatibility, when a Controller or Razor Pages endpoint delegate is executed, the properties of [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) are set to appropriate values based on the request processing performed thus far.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-303">Il tipo di `RouteContext` verrà contrassegnato come obsoleto in una versione futura:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-303">The `RouteContext` type will be marked obsolete in a future release:</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-304">Eseguire la migrazione `RouteData.Values` `HttpRequest.RouteValues`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-304">Migrate `RouteData.Values` to `HttpRequest.RouteValues`.</span></span>
> * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-305">Eseguire la migrazione `RouteData.DataTokens` per recuperare [IDataTokensMetadata](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IDataTokensMetadata) dai metadati dell'endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-305">Migrate `RouteData.DataTokens` to retrieve [IDataTokensMetadata](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IDataTokensMetadata) from the endpoint metadata.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-306">La corrispondenza degli URL opera in un set di fasi configurabile.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-306">URL matching operates in a configurable set of phases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-307">In ogni fase l'output è un set di corrispondenze.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-307">In each phase, the output is a set of matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-308">Il set di corrispondenze può essere ulteriormente ridotto dalla fase successiva.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-308">The set of matches can be narrowed down further by the next phase.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-309">L'implementazione del routing non garantisce un ordine di elaborazione per gli endpoint corrispondenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-309">The routing implementation does not guarantee a processing order for matching endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-310">**Tutte le** corrispondenze possibili vengono elaborate in una sola volta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-310">**All** possible matches are processed at once.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-311">Le fasi corrispondenti dell'URL si verificano nell'ordine seguente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-311">The URL matching phases occur in the following order.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-312">ASP.NET Core:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-312">ASP.NET Core:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3658d-313">Elabora il percorso URL rispetto al set di endpoint e ai relativi modelli di route, raccogliendo **tutte** le corrispondenze.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-313">Processes the URL path against the set of endpoints and their route templates, collecting **all** of the matches.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="3658d-314">Accetta l'elenco precedente e rimuove le corrispondenze che non riescono con i vincoli di route applicati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-314">Takes the preceding list and removes matches that fail with route constraints applied.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="3658d-315">Accetta l'elenco precedente e rimuove le corrispondenze che non superano il set di istanze di [MatcherPolicy](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.MatcherPolicy) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-315">Takes the preceding list and removes matches that fail the set of [MatcherPolicy](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.MatcherPolicy) instances.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="3658d-316">USA [EndpointSelector](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Matching.EndpointSelector) per prendere una decisione finale dall'elenco precedente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-316">Uses the [EndpointSelector](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Matching.EndpointSelector) to make a final decision from the preceding list.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-317">Per l'elenco degli endpoint viene assegnata la priorità in base a:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-317">The list of endpoints is prioritized according to:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-318">[RouteEndpoint. Order](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.Order*)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-318">The [RouteEndpoint.Order](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.Order*)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-319">[Precedenza del modello di route](#rtp)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-319">The [route template precedence](#rtp)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-320">Tutti gli endpoint corrispondenti vengono elaborati in ogni fase fino a quando non viene raggiunto il <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Matching.EndpointSelector>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-320">All matching endpoints are processed in each phase until the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Matching.EndpointSelector> is reached.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-321">Il `EndpointSelector` è la fase finale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-321">The `EndpointSelector` is the final phase.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-322">Viene scelto l'endpoint con la priorità più alta dalle corrispondenze come la migliore corrispondenza.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-322">It chooses the highest priority endpoint from the matches as the best match.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-323">Se sono presenti altre corrispondenze con la stessa priorità della corrispondenza migliore, viene generata un'eccezione di corrispondenza ambigua.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-323">If there are other matches with the same priority as the best match, an ambiguous match exception is thrown.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-324">La precedenza della route viene calcolata in base a un modello di route **più specifico** a cui viene assegnata una priorità più alta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-324">The route precedence is computed based on a **more specific** route template being given a higher priority.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-325">Si consideri, ad esempio, i modelli `/hello` e `/{message}`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-325">For example, consider the templates `/hello` and `/{message}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-326">Entrambe corrispondono al percorso URL `/hello`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-326">Both match the URL path `/hello`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-327">`/hello` è più specifico e pertanto con una priorità più elevata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-327">`/hello`  is more specific and therefore higher priority.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-328">In generale, la precedenza della route consente di scegliere la migliore corrispondenza per i tipi di schemi URL usati in pratica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-328">In general, route precedence does a good job of choosing the best match for the kinds of URL schemes used in practice.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-329">Utilizzare <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.Order> solo quando necessario per evitare ambiguità.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-329">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.Order> only when necessary to avoid an ambiguity.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-330">A causa dei tipi di estendibilità offerti dal routing, non è possibile che il sistema di routing calcoli in anticipo le route ambigue.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-330">Due to the kinds of extensibility provided by routing, it isn't possible for the routing system to compute ahead of time the ambiguous routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-331">Si consideri ad esempio i modelli di route `/{message:alpha}` e `/{message:int}`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-331">Consider an example such as the route templates `/{message:alpha}` and `/{message:int}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-332">Il vincolo `alpha` corrisponde solo ai caratteri alfabetici.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-332">The `alpha` constraint matches only alphabetic characters.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-333">Il vincolo `int` corrisponde solo ai numeri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-333">The `int` constraint matches only numbers.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-334">Questi modelli hanno la stessa precedenza di route, ma non esiste un singolo URL corrispondente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-334">These templates have the same route precedence, but there's no single URL they both match.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-335">Se il sistema di routing ha segnalato un errore di ambiguità all'avvio, blocca il caso d'uso valido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-335">If the routing system reported an ambiguity error at startup, it would block this valid use case.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
>
> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-336">L'ordine delle operazioni all'interno di <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> non influisce sul comportamento del routing, con un'eccezione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-336">The order of operations inside <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> doesn't influence the behavior of routing, with one exception.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-337"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllerRoute*> e <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MvcAreaRouteBuilderExtensions.MapAreaRoute*> assegnano automaticamente un valore di ordine ai rispettivi endpoint in base all'ordine in cui vengono richiamati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-337"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllerRoute*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MvcAreaRouteBuilderExtensions.MapAreaRoute*> automatically assign an order value to their endpoints based on the order they are invoked.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-338">Questo simula il comportamento a lungo termine dei controller senza che il sistema di routing fornisca le stesse garanzie delle implementazioni di routing precedenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-338">This simulates long-time behavior of controllers without the routing system providing the same guarantees as older routing implementations.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-339">Nell'implementazione legacy del routing, è possibile implementare l'estendibilità del routing che dipende dall'ordine in cui vengono elaborate le route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-339">In the legacy implementation of routing, it's possible to implement routing extensibility that has a dependency on the order in which routes are processed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-340">Routing degli endpoint in ASP.NET Core 3,0 e versioni successive:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-340">Endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 3.0 and later:</span></span>
> 
> * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-341">Non ha un concetto di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-341">Doesn't have a concept of routes.</span></span>
> * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-342">Non fornisce garanzie di ordinamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-342">Doesn't provide ordering guarantees.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-343">Tutti gli endpoint vengono elaborati contemporaneamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-343">All endpoints are processed at once.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-344">Se questo significa che si è bloccati usando il sistema di routing legacy, [aprire un problema di GitHub per assistenza](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/issues).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-344">If this means you're stuck using the legacy routing system, [open a GitHub issue for assistance](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/issues).</span></span>

<a name="rtp"></a>

### <a name="route-template-precedence-and-endpoint-selection-order"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-345">Ordine di precedenza e selezione degli endpoint del modello di route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-345">Route template precedence and endpoint selection order</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-346">La [precedenza del modello di route](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Template/RoutePrecedence.cs#L16) è un sistema che assegna a ogni modello di route un valore in base a quanto è specifico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-346">[Route template precedence](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Template/RoutePrecedence.cs#L16) is a system that assigns each route template a value based on how specific it is.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-347">Precedenza modello di route:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-347">Route template precedence:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-348">Evita la necessità di modificare l'ordine degli endpoint in casi comuni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-348">Avoids the need to adjust the order of endpoints in common cases.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-349">Tenta di trovare la corrispondenza con le aspettative comuni del comportamento di routing.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-349">Attempts to match the common-sense expectations of routing behavior.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-350">Si considerino, ad esempio, i modelli `/Products/List` e `/Products/{id}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-350">For example, consider templates `/Products/List` and `/Products/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-351">È ragionevole presupporre che `/Products/List` sia una corrispondenza migliore rispetto `/Products/{id}` per il percorso URL `/Products/List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-351">It would be reasonable to assume that `/Products/List` is a better match than `/Products/{id}` for the URL path `/Products/List`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-352">Il funziona perché il segmento letterale `/List` viene considerato con una precedenza migliore rispetto al segmento di parametro `/{id}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-352">The works because the literal segment `/List` is considered to have better precedence than the parameter segment `/{id}`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-353">I dettagli del funzionamento della precedenza sono associati alla modalità di definizione dei modelli di route:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-353">The details of how precedence works are coupled to how route templates are defined:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-354">I modelli con più segmenti sono considerati più specifici.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-354">Templates with more segments are considered more specific.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-355">Un segmento con testo letterale viene considerato più specifico rispetto a un segmento di parametro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-355">A segment with literal text is considered more specific than a parameter segment.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-356">Un segmento di parametro con un vincolo è considerato più specifico di uno senza.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-356">A parameter segment with a constraint is considered more specific than one without.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-357">Un segmento complesso è considerato specifico come un segmento di parametro con un vincolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-357">A complex segment is considered as specific as a parameter segment with a constraint.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-358">Catch all parameters è il meno specifico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-358">Catch all parameters are the least specific.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-359">Per un riferimento di valori esatti, vedere il [codice sorgente su GitHub](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Template/RoutePrecedence.cs#L189) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-359">See the [source code on GitHub](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Template/RoutePrecedence.cs#L189) for a reference of exact values.</span></span>

<a name="lg"></a>

### <a name="url-generation-concepts"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-360">Concetti relativi alla generazione di URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-360">URL generation concepts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-361">Generazione URL:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-361">URL generation:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-362">È il processo mediante il quale il routing può creare un percorso URL basato su un set di valori di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-362">Is the process by which routing can create a URL path based on a set of route values.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-363">Consente una separazione logica tra gli endpoint e gli URL che vi accedono.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-363">Allows for a logical separation between endpoints and the URLs that access them.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-364">Il routing degli endpoint include l'API <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-364">Endpoint routing includes the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-365">`LinkGenerator` è un servizio singleton disponibile in [di](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-365">`LinkGenerator` is a singleton service available from [DI](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-366">L'API `LinkGenerator` può essere usata al di fuori del contesto di una richiesta in esecuzione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-366">The `LinkGenerator` API can be used outside of the context of an executing request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-367">[MVC. IUrlHelper](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper) e scenari basati su <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>, ad esempio gli [Helper Tag](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro), gli helper HTML e [i risultati dell'azione](xref:mvc/controllers/actions), usano l'API `LinkGenerator` internamente per fornire funzionalità di generazione dei collegamenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-367">[Mvc.IUrlHelper](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper) and scenarios that rely on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>, such as [Tag Helpers](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro), HTML Helpers, and [Action Results](xref:mvc/controllers/actions), use the `LinkGenerator` API internally to provide link generating capabilities.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-368">Il generatore di collegamenti si basa sui concetti di **indirizzo** e di **schemi di indirizzi**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-368">The link generator is backed by the concept of an **address** and **address schemes**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-369">Lo schema di indirizzi consente di determinare gli endpoint che devono essere considerati per la generazione dei collegamenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-369">An address scheme is a way of determining the endpoints that should be considered for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-370">Ad esempio, il nome della route e gli scenari dei valori di route molti utenti hanno familiarità con i controller e Razor Pages vengono implementati come uno schema di indirizzi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-370">For example, the route name and route values scenarios many users are familiar with from controllers and Razor Pages are implemented as an address scheme.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-371">Il generatore di collegamenti può collegarsi ai controller e Razor Pages tramite i metodi di estensione seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-371">The link generator can link to controllers and Razor Pages via the following extension methods:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByPage*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByPage*>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-372">Gli overload di questi metodi accettano argomenti che includono la `HttpContext`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-372">Overloads of these methods accept arguments that include the `HttpContext`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-373">Questi metodi sono equivalenti dal punto di vista funzionale a [URL. Action](xref:System.Web.Mvc.UrlHelper.Action*) e [URL. Page](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.UrlHelperExtensions.Page*), ma offrono flessibilità e opzioni aggiuntive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-373">These methods are functionally equivalent to [Url.Action](xref:System.Web.Mvc.UrlHelper.Action*) and [Url.Page](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.UrlHelperExtensions.Page*), but offer additional flexibility and options.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-374">I `GetPath*` metodi sono molto simili a `Url.Action` e `Url.Page`, in quanto generano un URI contenente un percorso assoluto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-374">The `GetPath*` methods are most similar to `Url.Action` and `Url.Page`, in that they generate a URI containing an absolute path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-375">I metodi `GetUri*` generano sempre un URI assoluto contenente uno schema e un host.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-375">The `GetUri*` methods always generate an absolute URI containing a scheme and host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-376">I metodi che accettano `HttpContext` generano un URI nel contesto della richiesta in esecuzione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-376">The methods that accept an `HttpContext` generate a URI in the context of the executing request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-377">I valori della route di [ambiente](#ambient) , il percorso di base URL, lo schema e l'host dalla richiesta in esecuzione vengono usati a meno che non vengano sottoposti a override.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-377">The [ambient](#ambient) route values, URL base path, scheme, and host from the executing request are used unless overridden.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-378"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> viene chiamato con un indirizzo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-378"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> is called with an address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-379">La generazione di un URI viene eseguita in due passaggi:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-379">Generating a URI occurs in two steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3658d-380">Un indirizzo viene associato a un elenco di endpoint che corrispondono all'indirizzo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-380">An address is bound to a list of endpoints that match the address.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="3658d-381"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.RoutePattern> di ogni endpoint viene valutato fino a quando non viene individuato un formato di route che corrisponde ai valori specificati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-381">Each endpoint's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.RoutePattern> is evaluated until a route pattern that matches the supplied values is found.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-382">L'output risultante viene unito alle altre parti dell'URI specificate nel generatore di collegamenti e restituito.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-382">The resulting output is combined with the other URI parts supplied to the link generator and returned.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-383">I metodi forniti da <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> supportano le funzionalità di generazione di collegamenti standard per tutti i tipi di indirizzi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-383">The methods provided by <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> support standard link generation capabilities for any type of address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-384">Il modo più pratico per usare il generatore di collegamenti è tramite i metodi di estensione che eseguono operazioni per un tipo di indirizzo specifico:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-384">The most convenient way to use the link generator is through extension methods that perform operations for a specific address type:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="3658d-385">Metodo di estensione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-385">Extension Method</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-386">Descrizione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-386">Description</span></span> |
| ---------------- | ----------- |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-387">Genera un URI con un percorso assoluto in base ai valori specificati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-387">Generates a URI with an absolute path based on the provided values.</span></span> |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetUriByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-388">Genera un URI assoluto in base ai valori specificati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-388">Generates an absolute URI based on the provided values.</span></span>             |

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-389">Prestare attenzione alle implicazioni seguenti della chiamata ai metodi <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-389">Pay attention to the following implications of calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> methods:</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-390">Usare i metodi di estensione `GetUri*` con cautela in una configurazione di app che non convalida l'intestazione `Host` delle richieste in ingresso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-390">Use `GetUri*` extension methods with caution in an app configuration that doesn't validate the `Host` header of incoming requests.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-391">Se l'intestazione `Host` delle richieste in ingresso non viene convalidata, l'input della richiesta non attendibile può essere restituito al client negli URI in una vista o in una pagina.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-391">If the `Host` header of incoming requests isn't validated, untrusted request input can be sent back to the client in URIs in a view or page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-392">È consigliabile che in tutte le app di produzione il server sia configurato per la convalida dell'intestazione `Host` rispetto ai valori validi noti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-392">We recommend that all production apps configure their server to validate the `Host` header against known valid values.</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-393">Usare <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> con cautela nel middleware in associazione a `Map` o `MapWhen`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-393">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> with caution in middleware in combination with `Map` or `MapWhen`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-394">`Map*` modifica il percorso di base della richiesta in esecuzione, che ha effetto sull'output della generazione di collegamenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-394">`Map*` changes the base path of the executing request, which affects the output of link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-395">Tutte le API <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> consentono di specificare un percorso di base.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-395">All of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> APIs allow specifying a base path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-396">Specificare un percorso di base vuoto per annullare l'`Map*` effetti sulla generazione del collegamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-396">Specify an empty base path to undo the `Map*` affect on link generation.</span></span>

### <a name="middleware-example"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-397">Esempio di middleware</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-397">Middleware example</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-398">Nell'esempio seguente, un middleware usa l'API <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> per creare un collegamento a un metodo di azione che elenca i prodotti dell'archivio.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-398">In the following example, a middleware uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API to create a link to an action method that lists store products.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-399">Usando il generatore di collegamenti inserendolo in una classe e chiamando `GenerateLink` è disponibile per qualsiasi classe in un'app:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-399">Using the link generator by injecting it into a class and calling `GenerateLink` is available to any class in an app:</span></span>
