<a name="rtr"></a>

## <a name="route-template-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-400">Riferimento per il modello di route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-400">Route template reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-401">I token all'interno `{}` definiscono i parametri di route associati se la route viene confrontata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-401">Tokens within `{}` define route parameters that are bound if the route is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-402">È possibile definire più di un parametro di route in un segmento di route, ma i parametri di route devono essere separati da un valore letterale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-402">More than one route parameter can be defined in a route segment, but route parameters  must be separated by a literal value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-403">Ad esempio, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` non è una route valida perché non è presente un valore letterale tra `{controller}` e `{action}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-403">For example, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` isn't a valid route, since there's no literal value between `{controller}` and `{action}`.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="3658d-404">I parametri di route devono avere un nome e possono avere attributi aggiuntivi specificati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-404">Route parameters must have a name and may have additional attributes specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-405">Il testo letterale diverso dai parametri di route, ad esempio `{id}`, e il separatore di percorso `/` devono corrispondere al testo nell'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-405">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-406">La corrispondenza del testo non fa distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole e si basa sulla rappresentazione decodificata del percorso degli URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-406">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URLs path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-407">Per trovare la corrispondenza con un delimitatore di parametro di route letterale `{` o `}`, eseguire l'escape del delimitatore ripetendo il carattere.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-407">To match a literal route parameter delimiter `{` or `}`, escape the delimiter by repeating the character.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-408">Ad esempio `{{` o `}}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-408">For example `{{` or `}}`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-409">`**`asterisco `*` o Double asterisco:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-409">Asterisk `*` or double asterisk `**`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-410">Può essere usato come prefisso per un parametro di route per l'associazione al resto dell'URI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-410">Can be used as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-411">Sono detti parametri **catch-all** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-411">Are called a **catch-all** parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-412">Ad esempio, `blog/{**slug}`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-412">For example, `blog/{**slug}`:</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-413">Corrisponde a qualsiasi URI che inizia con `/blog` e ha un valore che lo segue.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-413">Matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-414">Il valore seguente `/blog` viene assegnato al valore di route [Slug](https://developer.mozilla.org/docs/Glossary/Slug) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-414">The value following `/blog` is assigned to the [slug](https://developer.mozilla.org/docs/Glossary/Slug) route value.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-415">I parametri catch-all possono anche corrispondere alla stringa vuota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-415">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-416">Il parametro catch-all esegue l'escape dei caratteri appropriati quando la route viene usata per generare un URL, incluso il separatore di percorso `/` caratteri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-416">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator `/` characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-417">Ad esempio, la route `foo/{*path}` con i valori di route `{ path = "my/path" }` genera `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-417">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-418">Si noti la barra di escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-418">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-419">Per eseguire il round trip dei caratteri di separatore di percorso, usare il prefisso del parametro di route `**`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-419">To round-trip path separator characters, use the `**` route parameter prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-420">La route `foo/{**path}` con `{ path = "my/path" }` genera `foo/my/path`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-420">The route `foo/{**path}` with `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my/path`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-421">I modelli di URL che tentano di acquisire un nome file con un'estensione facoltativa hanno considerazioni aggiuntive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-421">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-422">Considerare ad esempio il modello `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-422">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-423">Se esistono i valori per `filename` e `ext`, vengono popolati entrambi i valori.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-423">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-424">Se nell'URL è presente solo un valore per `filename`, la route corrisponde perché la `.` finale è facoltativa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-424">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing `.` is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-425">Gli URL seguenti corrispondono a questa route:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-425">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-426">I parametri di route possono avere **valori predefiniti**, definiti specificando il valore predefinito dopo il nome del parametro, separato da un segno di uguale (`=`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-426">Route parameters may have **default values** designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-427">Ad esempio, `{controller=Home}` definisce `Home` come valore predefinito per `controller`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-427">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-428">Il valore predefinito viene usato se nell'URL non è presente alcun valore per il parametro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-428">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-429">I parametri di route vengono resi facoltativi aggiungendo un punto interrogativo (`?`) alla fine del nome del parametro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-429">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-430">Ad esempio: `id?`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-430">For example, `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-431">La differenza tra i valori facoltativi e i parametri di route predefiniti è la seguente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-431">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-432">Un parametro di route con un valore predefinito produce sempre un valore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-432">A route parameter with a default value always produces a value.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-433">Un parametro facoltativo ha un valore solo quando un valore viene fornito dall'URL della richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-433">An optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-434">I parametri di route possono presentare dei vincoli che devono corrispondere al valore di route associato dall'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-434">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-435">Se si aggiunge `:` e il nome del vincolo dopo il nome del parametro di route, viene specificato un vincolo inline in un parametro di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-435">Adding `:` and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an inline constraint on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-436">Se il vincolo richiede argomenti, vengono racchiusi tra parentesi `(...)` dopo il nome del vincolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-436">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses `(...)` after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-437">È possibile specificare più *vincoli inline* accodando un altro `:` e il nome del vincolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-437">Multiple *inline constraints* can be specified by appending another `:` and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-438">Il nome del vincolo e gli argomenti vengono passati al servizio <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> per creare un'istanza di <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> da usare nell'elaborazione dell'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-438">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-439">Il modello di route `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifica ad esempio un vincolo `minlength` con l'argomento `10`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-439">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-440">Per altre informazioni sui vincoli di route e per un elenco dei vincoli specificati dal framework, vedere la sezione [Riferimento per i vincoli di route](#route-constraint-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-440">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-441">I parametri di route possono avere anche trasformatori di parametro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-441">Route parameters may also have parameter transformers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-442">I trasformatori di parametro trasformano il valore di un parametro durante la generazione di collegamenti, azioni e pagine corrispondenti agli URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-442">Parameter transformers transform a parameter's value when generating links and matching actions and pages to URLs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-443">Analogamente ai vincoli, i trasformatori di parametro possono essere aggiunti inline a un parametro di route aggiungendo un `:` e il nome del trasformatore dopo il nome del parametro di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-443">Like constraints, parameter transformers can be added inline to a route parameter by adding a `:` and transformer name after the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-444">Ad esempio, il modello di route `blog/{article:slugify}` specifica un trasformatore `slugify`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-444">For example, the route template `blog/{article:slugify}` specifies a `slugify` transformer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-445">Per altre informazioni sui trasformatori di parametro, vedere la sezione [Riferimento ai trasformatori di parametro](#parameter-transformer-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-445">For more information on parameter transformers, see the [Parameter transformer reference](#parameter-transformer-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-446">La tabella seguente illustra i modelli di route di esempio e il relativo comportamento:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-446">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="3658d-447">Modello di route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-447">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-448">URI corrispondente di esempio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-448">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-449">L'URI della richiesta&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-449">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-450">Verifica la corrispondenza solo del singolo percorso `/hello`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-450">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-451">Verifica la corrispondenza e imposta `Page` su `Home`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-451">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-452">Verifica la corrispondenza e imposta `Page` su `Contact`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-452">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-453">Esegue il mapping al controller `Products` e all'azione `List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-453">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-454">Esegue il mapping al controller `Products` e `Details` azione con`id` impostata su 123.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-454">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action with`id` set to 123.</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-455">Esegue il mapping al controller `Home` e al metodo `Index`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-455">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-456">`id` viene ignorato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-456">`id` is ignored.</span></span>        |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/Products`         | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-457">Esegue il mapping al controller `Products` e al metodo `Index`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-457">Maps to the `Products` controller and `Index` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-458">`id` viene ignorato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-458">`id` is ignored.</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-459">L'uso di un modello è in genere l'approccio più semplice al routing.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-459">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-460">I vincoli e le impostazioni predefinite possono essere specificati anche all'esterno del modello di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-460">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

### <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-461">Segmenti complessi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-461">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-462">I segmenti complessi vengono elaborati mediante la corrispondenza di delimitatori letterali da destra a sinistra in modo [non greedy](#greedy) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-462">Complex segments are processed by matching up literal delimiters from right to left in a [non-greedy](#greedy) way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-463">`[Route("/a{b}c{d}")]` è ad esempio un segmento complesso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-463">For example, `[Route("/a{b}c{d}")]` is a complex segment.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="3658d-464">I segmenti complessi funzionano in un modo specifico che devono essere riconosciuti per utilizzarli correttamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-464">Complex segments work in a particular way that must be understood to use them successfully.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-465">Nell'esempio riportato in questa sezione viene illustrato il motivo per cui i segmenti complessi funzionano correttamente solo quando il testo del delimitatore non viene visualizzato all'interno dei valori del parametro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-465">The example in this section demonstrates why complex segments only really work well when the delimiter text doesn't appear inside the parameter values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-466">Per i casi più complessi, è necessario utilizzare un' [espressione regolare](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expressions) e quindi estrarre manualmente i valori.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-466">Using a [regex](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expressions) and then manually extracting the values is needed for more complex cases.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-467">Questo è un riepilogo dei passaggi eseguiti dal routing con il modello `/a{b}c{d}` e il percorso URL `/abcd`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-467">This is a summary of the steps that routing performs with the template `/a{b}c{d}` and the URL path `/abcd`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-468">Il `|` viene usato per semplificare la visualizzazione del funzionamento dell'algoritmo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-468">The `|` is used to help visualize how the algorithm works:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-469">Il primo valore letterale, da destra a sinistra, è `c`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-469">The first literal, right to left, is `c`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-470">Quindi `/abcd` viene eseguita una ricerca da destra e trova `/ab|c|d`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-470">So `/abcd` is searched from right and finds `/ab|c|d`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-471">Tutte le operazioni a destra (`d`) sono ora abbinate al parametro di route `{d}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-471">Everything to the right (`d`) is now matched to the route parameter `{d}`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-472">Il valore letterale successivo, da destra a sinistra, è `a`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-472">The next literal, right to left, is `a`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-473">Quindi `/ab|c|d` viene eseguita una ricerca a partire dal punto in cui è stata interrotta, `a` viene trovato `/|a|b|c|d`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-473">So `/ab|c|d` is searched starting where we left off, then `a` is found `/|a|b|c|d`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-474">Il valore a destra (`b`) viene ora associato al parametro di route `{b}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-474">The value to the right (`b`) is now matched to the route parameter `{b}`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-475">Non esiste alcun testo rimanente e nessun modello di route rimanente, quindi si tratta di una corrispondenza.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-475">There is no remaining text and no remaining route template, so this is a match.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-476">Di seguito è riportato un esempio di un caso negativo che usa lo stesso modello `/a{b}c{d}` e il percorso URL `/aabcd`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-476">Here's an example of a negative case using the same template `/a{b}c{d}` and the URL path `/aabcd`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-477">Il `|` viene usato per semplificare la visualizzazione del funzionamento dell'algoritmo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-477">The `|` is used to help visualize how the algorithm works.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-478">Questo caso non corrisponde a una corrispondenza, descritta dallo stesso algoritmo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-478">This case isn't a match, which is explained by the same algorithm:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-479">Il primo valore letterale, da destra a sinistra, è `c`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-479">The first literal, right to left, is `c`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-480">Quindi `/aabcd` viene eseguita una ricerca da destra e trova `/aab|c|d`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-480">So `/aabcd` is searched from right and finds `/aab|c|d`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-481">Tutte le operazioni a destra (`d`) sono ora abbinate al parametro di route `{d}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-481">Everything to the right (`d`) is now matched to the route parameter `{d}`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-482">Il valore letterale successivo, da destra a sinistra, è `a`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-482">The next literal, right to left, is `a`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-483">Quindi `/aab|c|d` viene eseguita una ricerca a partire dal punto in cui è stata interrotta, `a` viene trovato `/a|a|b|c|d`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-483">So `/aab|c|d` is searched starting where we left off, then `a` is found `/a|a|b|c|d`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-484">Il valore a destra (`b`) viene ora associato al parametro di route `{b}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-484">The value to the right (`b`) is now matched to the route parameter `{b}`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-485">A questo punto il testo rimanente `a`, ma l'algoritmo ha esaurito il modello di route da analizzare, quindi non si tratta di una corrispondenza.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-485">At this point there is remaining text `a`, but the algorithm has run out of route template to parse, so this is not a match.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-486">Poiché l'algoritmo di corrispondenza [non è greedy](#greedy):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-486">Since the matching algorithm is [non-greedy](#greedy):</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-487">Corrisponde alla minima quantità di testo possibile in ogni passaggio.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-487">It matches the smallest amount of text possible in each step.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-488">Ogni caso in cui il valore del delimitatore viene visualizzato all'interno dei valori del parametro non corrisponde.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-488">Any case where the delimiter value appears inside the parameter values results in not matching.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-489">Le espressioni regolari forniscono un maggiore controllo sul comportamento corrispondente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-489">Regular expressions provide much more control over their matching behavior.</span></span>

<a name="greedy"></a>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-490">La corrispondenza greedy, conosciuta anche come [Corrispondenza Lazy](https://wikipedia.org/wiki/Regular_expression#Lazy_matching), corrisponde alla stringa più grande possibile.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-490">Greedy matching, also know as [lazy matching](https://wikipedia.org/wiki/Regular_expression#Lazy_matching), matches the largest possible string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-491">Non greedy corrisponde alla stringa più piccola possibile.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-491">Non-greedy matches the smallest possible string.</span></span>

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-492">Riferimento per i vincoli di route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-492">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-493">I vincoli di route vengono eseguiti quando si verifica una corrispondenza nell'URL in ingresso e il percorso URL viene suddiviso in valori di route in formato token.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-493">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-494">I vincoli di route controllano in genere il valore di route associato tramite il modello di route e fanno una decisione vera o falsa sul fatto che il valore sia accettabile.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-494">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a true or false decision about whether the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-495">Alcuni vincoli di route usano i dati all'esterno del valore di route per stabilire se la richiesta può essere instradata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-495">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-496">Ad esempio, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> può accettare o rifiutare una richiesta in base al relativo verbo HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-496">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-497">I vincoli vengono usati nelle richieste del routing e nella generazione di collegamenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-497">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-498">Non usare vincoli per la convalida dell'input.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-498">Don't use constraints for input validation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-499">Se vengono usati vincoli per la convalida dell'input, l'input non valido restituisce una risposta `404` non trovata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-499">If constraints are used for input validation, invalid input results in a `404` Not Found response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-500">L'input non valido deve produrre una richiesta `400` non valida con un messaggio di errore appropriato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-500">Invalid input should produce a `400` Bad Request with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-501">I vincoli di route vengono usati per evitare ambiguità nelle route simili e non per convalidare gli input per una route specifica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-501">Route constraints are used to disambiguate similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-502">La tabella seguente illustra i vincoli di route di esempio e il comportamento previsto:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-502">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="3658d-503">vincolo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-503">constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-504">Esempio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-504">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-505">Esempi di corrispondenza</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-505">Example Matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-506">Note</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-506">Notes</span></span> |
| ---------- | ------- | --------------- | ----- |
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-507">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-507">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-508">Corrisponde a qualsiasi numero intero</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-508">Matches any integer</span></span> |
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-509">`true`, `FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-509">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-510">Corrisponde `true` o `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-510">Matches `true` or `false`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-511">Non fa distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-511">Case-insensitive</span></span> |
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-512">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-512">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-513">Corrisponde a un valore `DateTime` valido nella lingua inglese.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-513">Matches a valid `DateTime` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-514">Vedere l'avviso precedente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-514">See preceding warning.</span></span> |
| `decimal` | `{price:decimal}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-515">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-515">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-516">Corrisponde a un valore `decimal` valido nella lingua inglese.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-516">Matches a valid `decimal` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-517">Vedere l'avviso precedente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-517">See preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `double` | `{weight:double}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-518">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-518">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-519">Corrisponde a un valore `double` valido nella lingua inglese.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-519">Matches a valid `double` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-520">Vedere l'avviso precedente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-520">See preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `float` | `{weight:float}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-521">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-521">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-522">Corrisponde a un valore `float` valido nella lingua inglese.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-522">Matches a valid `float` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-523">Vedere l'avviso precedente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-523">See preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `guid` | `{id:guid}` | `CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-524">Corrisponde a un valore `Guid` valido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-524">Matches a valid `Guid` value</span></span> |
| `long` | `{ticks:long}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-525">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-525">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-526">Corrisponde a un valore `long` valido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-526">Matches a valid `long` value</span></span> |
| `minlength(value)` | `{username:minlength(4)}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-527">La stringa deve contenere almeno 4 caratteri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-527">String must be at least 4 characters</span></span> |
| `maxlength(value)` | `{filename:maxlength(8)}` | `MyFile` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-528">La stringa non deve contenere più di 8 caratteri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-528">String must be no more than 8 characters</span></span> |
| `length(length)` | `{filename:length(12)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-529">La stringa deve contenere esattamente 12 caratteri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-529">String must be exactly 12 characters long</span></span> |
| `length(min,max)` | `{filename:length(8,16)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-530">La stringa deve contenere almeno 8 e non più di 16 caratteri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-530">String must be at least 8 and no more than 16 characters long</span></span> |
| `min(value)` | `{age:min(18)}` | `19` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-531">Il valore intero deve essere almeno 18</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-531">Integer value must be at least 18</span></span> |
| `max(value)` | `{age:max(120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-532">Il valore intero non deve essere superiore a 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-532">Integer value must be no more than 120</span></span> |
| `range(min,max)` | `{age:range(18,120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-533">Il valore intero deve essere almeno 18 ma non più di 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-533">Integer value must be at least 18 but no more than 120</span></span> |
| `alpha` | `{name:alpha}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-534">La stringa deve essere costituita da uno o più caratteri alfabetici, `a`-`z` e senza distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-534">String must consist of one or more alphabetical characters, `a`-`z` and case-insensitive.</span></span> |
| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-535">La stringa deve corrispondere all'espressione regolare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-535">String must match the regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-536">Vedere suggerimenti sulla definizione di un'espressione regolare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-536">See tips about defining a regular expression.</span></span> |
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-537">Usato per imporre che un valore diverso da un parametro sia presente durante la generazione dell'URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-537">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation</span></span> |

[!INCLUDE[](~/includes/regex.md)]

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-538">È possibile applicare più vincoli delimitati da due punti a un singolo parametro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-538">Multiple, colon delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-539">Ad esempio il vincolo seguente limita un parametro a un valore intero maggiore o uguale a 1:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-539">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-540">I vincoli di route che verificano l'URL e vengono convertiti in un tipo CLR utilizzano sempre la lingua inglese.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-540">Route constraints that verify the URL and are converted to a CLR type always use the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-541">Ad esempio, la conversione nel tipo CLR `int` o `DateTime`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-541">For example, conversion to the CLR type `int` or `DateTime`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-542">Questi vincoli presuppongono che l'URL non sia localizzabile.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-542">These constraints assume that the URL is not localizable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-543">I vincoli di route specificati dal framework non modificano i valori archiviati nei valori di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-543">The framework-provided route constraints don't modify the values stored in route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-544">Tutti i valori di route analizzati dall'URL vengono archiviati come stringhe.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-544">All route values parsed from the URL are stored as strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-545">Ad esempio, il vincolo `float` prova a convertire il valore di route in un valore float, ma il valore convertito viene usato solo per verificare che può essere convertito in un valore float.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-545">For example, the `float` constraint attempts to convert the route value to a float, but the converted value is used only to verify it can be converted to a float.</span></span>

### <a name="regular-expressions-in-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-546">Espressioni regolari nei vincoli</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-546">Regular expressions in constraints</span></span>

[!INCLUDE[](~/includes/regex.md)]

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-547">Le espressioni regolari possono essere specificate come vincoli inline usando il vincolo di route `regex(...)`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-547">Regular expressions can be specified as inline constraints using the `regex(...)` route constraint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-548">I metodi nella famiglia di <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllerRoute*> accettano anche un valore letterale di oggetti Constraints.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-548">Methods in the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllerRoute*> family also accept an object literal of constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-549">Se viene usato questo formato, i valori stringa vengono interpretati come espressioni regolari.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-549">If that form is used, string values are interpreted as regular expressions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-550">Il codice seguente usa un vincolo Regex inline:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-550">The following code uses an inline regex constraint:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-552">Il framework di ASP.NET Core aggiunge `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` al costruttore di espressioni regolari.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-552">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-553">Per una descrizione di questi membri, vedere <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-553">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-554">Le espressioni regolari usano delimitatori e token simili a quelli usati dal routing e dal C# linguaggio.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-554">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-555">Per i token di espressione è necessario aggiungere caratteri di escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-555">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-556">Per utilizzare l'espressione regolare `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in un vincolo inline, utilizzare uno dei seguenti elementi:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-556">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in an inline constraint, use one of the following:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-557">Sostituire `\` caratteri specificati nella stringa come `\\` caratteri nel file di C# origine per poter eseguire l'escape del carattere di escape `\` stringa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-557">Replace `\` characters provided in the string as `\\` characters in the C# source file in order to escape the `\` string escape character.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-558">[Valori letterali stringa Verbatim](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-558">[Verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-559">Per eseguire l'escape dei caratteri di delimitazione del parametro di routing `{`, `}`, `[``]`, raddoppiare i caratteri nell'espressione, ad esempio `{{`, `}}`, `[[``]]`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-559">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters `{`, `}`, `[`, `]`, double the characters in the expression, for example, `{{`, `}}`, `[[`, `]]`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-560">La tabella seguente illustra un'espressione regolare e la relativa versione di escape:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-560">The following table shows a regular expression and its escaped version:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="3658d-561">Espressione regolare‏</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-561">Regular expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-562">Espressione regolare con escape</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-562">Escaped regular expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-563">Le espressioni regolari utilizzate nel routing spesso iniziano con il carattere `^` e corrispondono alla posizione iniziale della stringa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-563">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the `^` character and match the starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-564">Le espressioni terminano spesso con il carattere `$` e corrispondono alla fine della stringa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-564">The expressions often end with the `$` character and match the end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-565">I caratteri `^` e `$` assicurano che l'espressione regolare corrisponda all'intero valore del parametro di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-565">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression matches the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-566">Senza i caratteri `^` e `$`, l'espressione regolare corrisponde a qualsiasi sottostringa all'interno della stringa, che è spesso indesiderata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-566">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression matches any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-567">La tabella seguente fornisce esempi e spiega perché corrispondono o non riescono a corrispondere:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-567">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="3658d-568">Expression</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-568">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-569">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-569">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-570">Corrispondente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-570">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-571">Commento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-571">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-572">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-572">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-573">Sì</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-573">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-574">Corrispondenze di sottostringhe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-574">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-575">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-575">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-576">Sì</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-576">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-577">Corrispondenze di sottostringhe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-577">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-578">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-578">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-579">Sì</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-579">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-580">Corrisponde all'espressione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-580">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-581">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-581">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-582">Sì</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-582">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-583">Senza distinzione maiuscole/minuscole</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-583">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-584">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-584">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-585">No</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-585">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-586">Vedere `^` e `$` sopra</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-586">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-587">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-587">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-588">No</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-588">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-589">Vedere `^` e `$` sopra</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-589">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-590">Per altre informazioni sulla sintassi delle espressioni regolari, vedere [Espressioni regolari di .NET Framework](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-590">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-591">Per limitare un parametro a un set noto di valori possibili, usare un'espressione regolare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-591">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-592">Ad esempio, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` verifica la corrispondenza del valore di route `action` solo con `list`, `get` o `create`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-592">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-593">Se viene passata nel dizionario di vincoli, la stringa `^(list|get|create)$` è equivalente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-593">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-594">Anche i vincoli passati nel dizionario dei vincoli che non corrispondono a uno dei vincoli noti vengono considerati espressioni regolari.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-594">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-595">I vincoli passati in un modello che non corrispondono a uno dei vincoli noti non vengono considerati come espressioni regolari.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-595">Constraints that are passed  within a template that don't match one of the known constraints are not treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

### <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-596">Vincoli di Route personalizzati</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-596">Custom route constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-597">È possibile creare vincoli di Route personalizzati implementando l'interfaccia <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-597">Custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-598">L'interfaccia `IRouteConstraint` contiene <xref:System.Web.Routing.IRouteConstraint.Match*>, che restituisce `true` se il vincolo viene soddisfatto e `false` in caso contrario.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-598">The `IRouteConstraint` interface contains <xref:System.Web.Routing.IRouteConstraint.Match*>, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-599">I vincoli di Route personalizzati sono raramente necessari.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-599">Custom route constraints are rarely needed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-600">Prima di implementare un vincolo di route personalizzato, prendere in considerazione le alternative, ad esempio l'associazione di modelli.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-600">Before implementing a custom route constraint, consider alternatives, such as model binding.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-601">Per usare un `IRouteConstraint`personalizzato, il tipo di vincolo di route deve essere registrato con l'<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> dell'app nel contenitore dei servizi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-601">To use a custom `IRouteConstraint`, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-602">`ConstraintMap` è un dizionario che esegue il mapping delle chiavi dei vincoli di route alle implementazioni di `IRouteConstraint` che convalidano tali vincoli.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-602">A `ConstraintMap` is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to `IRouteConstraint` implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-603">La proprietà `ConstraintMap` di un'app può essere aggiornata in `Startup.ConfigureServices` come parte di una chiamata [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) o configurando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> direttamente con `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-603">An app's `ConstraintMap` can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-604">Ad esempio,</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-604">For example:</span></span>

## <a name="parameter-transformer-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-616">Riferimento ai trasformatori di parametro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-616">Parameter transformer reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-617">I trasformatori di parametro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-617">Parameter transformers:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-618">Eseguire quando si genera un collegamento utilizzando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-618">Execute when generating a link using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-619">Implementare <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer?displayProperty=fullName>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-619">Implement <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer?displayProperty=fullName>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-620">Vengono configurati tramite <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-620">Are configured using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-621">Acquisire il valore della route del parametro e trasformarlo in un nuovo valore stringa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-621">Take the parameter's route value and transform it to a new string value.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-622">Il valore trasformato viene usato nel collegamento generato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-622">Result in using the transformed value in the generated link.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-623">Ad esempio, un trasformatore di parametro `slugify` personalizzato nel modello di route `blog\{article:slugify}` con `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` genera `blog\my-test-article`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-623">For example, a custom `slugify` parameter transformer in route pattern `blog\{article:slugify}` with `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` generates `blog\my-test-article`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-626">Il framework ASP.NET Core usa i trasformatori di parametro per trasformare l'URI in cui viene risolto un endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-626">The ASP.NET Core framework uses parameter transformers to transform the URI where an endpoint resolves.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-627">I trasformatori dei parametri, ad esempio, trasformano i valori di route utilizzati per la corrispondenza di un `area`, `controller`, `action`e `page`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-627">For example, parameter transformers transform the route values used to match an `area`, `controller`, `action`, and `page`.</span></span>

routes.MapControllerRoute(

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-631">ASP.NET Core fornisce le convenzioni API per l'uso di trasformatori di parametri con route generate:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-631">ASP.NET Core provides API conventions for using parameter transformers with generated routes:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-632">La convenzione <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention?displayProperty=fullName> MVC applica un trasformatore di parametro specificato a tutte le route di attributi nell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-632">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention?displayProperty=fullName> MVC convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all attribute routes in the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-633">Il trasformatore di parametro trasforma i token di route di attributi man mano che vengono sostituiti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-633">The parameter transformer transforms attribute route tokens as they are replaced.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-634">Per altre informazioni vedere [Use a parameter transformer to customize token replacement](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement) (Usare un trasformatore di parametro per personalizzare la sostituzione di token).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-634">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize token replacement](xref:mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-635">Razor Pages usa la convenzione API <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-635">Razor Pages uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention> API convention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-636">Questa convenzione applica un trasformatore di parametro specificato a tutte le istanze di Razor Pages individuate automaticamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-636">This convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all automatically discovered Razor Pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-637">Il trasformatore di parametro trasforma la cartella e i segmenti di nome file delle route di Razor Pages.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-637">The parameter transformer transforms the folder and file name segments of Razor Pages routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-638">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Use a parameter transformer to customize page routes](xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes) (Usare un trasformatore di parametro per personalizzare route di pagine).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-638">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize page routes](xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes).</span></span>

<a name="ugr"></a>

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-639">Riferimento per la generazione di URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-639">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-640">Questa sezione contiene un riferimento per l'algoritmo implementato dalla generazione di URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-640">This section contains a reference for the algorithm implemented by URL generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-641">In pratica, gli esempi più complessi di generazione di URL usano controller o Razor Pages.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-641">In practice, most complex examples of URL generation use controllers or Razor Pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-642">Per ulteriori informazioni, vedere [routing nei controller](xref:mvc/controllers/routing) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-642">See  [routing in controllers](xref:mvc/controllers/routing) for additional information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-643">Il processo di generazione dell'URL inizia con una chiamata a [LinkGenerator. GetPathByAddress](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress*) o a un metodo simile.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-643">The URL generation process begins with a call to [LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress*) or a similar method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-644">Il metodo viene fornito con un indirizzo, un set di valori di route e, facoltativamente, informazioni sulla richiesta corrente da `HttpContext`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-644">The method is provided with an address, a set of route values, and optionally information about the current request from `HttpContext`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-645">Il primo passaggio consiste nell'usare l'indirizzo per risolvere un set di endpoint candidati usando un [`IEndpointAddressScheme<TAddress>`](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointAddressScheme`1) corrispondente al tipo dell'indirizzo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-645">The first step is to use the address to resolve a set of candidate endpoints using an [`IEndpointAddressScheme<TAddress>`](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointAddressScheme`1) that matches the address's type.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-646">Una volta che il set di candidati è stato trovato dallo schema degli indirizzi, gli endpoint vengono ordinati ed elaborati in modo iterativo fino a quando un'operazione di generazione URL non riesce.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-646">Once of set of candidates is found by the address scheme, the endpoints are ordered and processed iteratively until a URL generation operation succeeds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-647">La generazione di URL **non** controlla le ambiguità, il primo risultato restituito è il risultato finale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-647">URL generation does **not** check for ambiguities, the first result returned is the final result.</span></span>

### <a name="troubleshooting-url-generation-with-logging"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-648">Risoluzione dei problemi di generazione URL con registrazione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-648">Troubleshooting URL generation with logging</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-649">Il primo passaggio nella risoluzione dei problemi di generazione degli URL consiste nell'impostazione del livello di registrazione di `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing` su `TRACE`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-649">The first step in troubleshooting URL generation is setting the logging level of `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing` to `TRACE`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-650">`LinkGenerator` registra molti dettagli sull'elaborazione che possono essere utili per la risoluzione dei problemi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-650">`LinkGenerator` logs many details about its processing which can be useful to troubleshoot problems.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-651">Per informazioni dettagliate sulla generazione di URL, vedere riferimento per la [generazione di URL](#ugr) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-651">See [URL generation reference](#ugr) for details on URL generation.</span></span>

### <a name="addresses"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-652">Indirizzi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-652">Addresses</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-653">Gli indirizzi rappresentano il concetto di generazione di URL usato per associare una chiamata al generatore di collegamenti a un set di endpoint candidati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-653">Addresses are the concept in URL generation used to bind a call into the link generator to a set of candidate endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-654">Gli indirizzi sono un concetto estendibile che include due implementazioni per impostazione predefinita:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-654">Addresses are an extensible concept that come with two implementations by default:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-655">Utilizzando il *nome dell'endpoint* (`string`) come indirizzo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-655">Using *endpoint name* (`string`) as the address:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-656">Fornisce funzionalità simili al nome della route MVC.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-656">Provides similar functionality to MVC's route name.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-657">Usa il tipo di metadati <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointNameMetadata>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-657">Uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointNameMetadata> metadata type.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-658">Risolve la stringa fornita in base ai metadati di tutti gli endpoint registrati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-658">Resolves the provided string against the metadata of all registered endpoints.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-659">Genera un'eccezione all'avvio se più endpoint utilizzano lo stesso nome.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-659">Throws an exception on startup if multiple endpoints use the same name.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-660">Consigliato per uso generico all'esterno dei controller e Razor Pages.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-660">Recommended for general-purpose use outside of controllers and Razor Pages.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-661">Utilizzando *i valori di route* (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteValuesAddress>) come indirizzo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-661">Using *route values* (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteValuesAddress>) as the address:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-662">Fornisce funzionalità simili ai controller e Razor Pages generazione di URL legacy.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-662">Provides similar functionality to controllers and Razor Pages legacy URL generation.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-663">Molto complesso da estendere ed eseguire il debug.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-663">Very complex to extend and debug.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-664">Fornisce l'implementazione utilizzata da `IUrlHelper`, helper tag, helper HTML, risultati dell'azione e così via.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-664">Provides the implementation used by `IUrlHelper`, Tag Helpers, HTML Helpers, Action Results, etc.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-665">Il ruolo dello schema di indirizzi è quello di fare in modo che l'associazione tra l'indirizzo e gli endpoint corrispondenti venga stabilita da criteri arbitrari:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-665">The role of the address scheme is to make the association between the address and matching endpoints by arbitrary criteria:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-666">Lo schema nome endpoint esegue una ricerca dizionario di base.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-666">The endpoint name scheme performs a basic dictionary lookup.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-667">Lo schema dei valori di route ha un subset migliore complesso di algoritmo set.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-667">The route values scheme has a complex best subset of set algorithm.</span></span>

<a name="ambient"></a>

### <a name="ambient-values-and-explicit-values"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-668">Valori di ambiente e valori espliciti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-668">Ambient values and explicit values</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-669">Dalla richiesta corrente, il routing accede ai valori della route della richiesta corrente `HttpContext.Request.RouteValues`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-669">From the current request, routing accesses the route values of the current request `HttpContext.Request.RouteValues`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-670">I valori associati alla richiesta corrente sono detti **valori di ambiente**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-670">The values associated with the current request are referred to as the **ambient values**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-671">Per maggiore chiarezza, la documentazione fa riferimento ai valori di route passati ai metodi come **valori espliciti**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-671">For the purpose of clarity, the documentation refers to the route values passed in to methods as **explicit values**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-672">Nell'esempio seguente vengono illustrati i valori di ambiente e i valori espliciti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-672">The following example shows ambient values and explicit values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-673">Fornisce valori di ambiente dalla richiesta corrente e dai valori espliciti: `{ id = 17, }`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-673">It provides ambient values from the current request and explicit values: `{ id = 17, }`:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/Controllers/WidgetController.cs?name=snippet)]

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-682">viene restituito `/Gadget/Edit/17`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-682">`/Gadget/Edit/17` is returned.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-683"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ControllerBase.Url> Ottiene l'<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-683"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ControllerBase.Url> gets the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-686">Il codice seguente fornisce valori di ambiente dalla richiesta corrente e dai valori espliciti: `{ page = "./Edit, id = 17, }`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-686">The following code provides ambient values from the current request and explicit values: `{ page = "./Edit, id = 17, }`:</span></span>
