<span data-ttu-id="3658d-947">Il generatore di collegamenti si basa sui concetti di *indirizzo* e di *schemi di indirizzi*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-947">The link generator is backed by the concept of an *address* and *address schemes*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-948">Lo schema di indirizzi consente di determinare gli endpoint che devono essere considerati per la generazione dei collegamenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-948">An address scheme is a way of determining the endpoints that should be considered for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-949">Ad esempio, gli scenari di nome route e valori di route noti a numerosi utenti in MVC o Razor Pages vengono implementati come schema di indirizzi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-949">For example, the route name and route values scenarios many users are familiar with from MVC/Razor Pages are implemented as an address scheme.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-950">Il generatore di collegamenti può collegarsi alle azioni e alle pagine MVC o Razor Pages tramite i metodi di estensione seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-950">The link generator can link to MVC/Razor Pages actions and pages via the following extension methods:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByPage*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByPage*>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-951">Un overload di questi metodi accetta gli argomenti che includono `HttpContext`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-951">An overload of these methods accepts arguments that include the `HttpContext`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-952">Questi metodi sono funzionalmente equivalenti a `Url.Action` e `Url.Page` ma offrono una maggiore flessibilità e altre opzioni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-952">These methods are functionally equivalent to `Url.Action` and `Url.Page` but offer additional flexibility and options.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-953">I metodi `GetPath*` sono più simili a `Url.Action` e `Url.Page` poiché generano un URI che contiene un percorso assoluto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-953">The `GetPath*` methods are most similar to `Url.Action` and `Url.Page` in that they generate a URI containing an absolute path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-954">I metodi `GetUri*` generano sempre un URI assoluto contenente uno schema e un host.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-954">The `GetUri*` methods always generate an absolute URI containing a scheme and host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-955">I metodi che accettano `HttpContext` generano un URI nel contesto della richiesta in esecuzione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-955">The methods that accept an `HttpContext` generate a URI in the context of the executing request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-956">Se non vengono sovrascritti, vengono usati i valori di route di ambiente, il percorso base dell'URL, lo schema e l'host dalla richiesta in esecuzione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-956">The ambient route values, URL base path, scheme, and host from the executing request are used unless overridden.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-957"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> viene chiamato con un indirizzo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-957"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> is called with an address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-958">La generazione di un URI viene eseguita in due passaggi:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-958">Generating a URI occurs in two steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3658d-959">Un indirizzo viene associato a un elenco di endpoint che corrispondono all'indirizzo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-959">An address is bound to a list of endpoints that match the address.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="3658d-960">`RoutePattern` di ogni endpoint viene valutato fino a quando non viene individuato un formato di route che corrisponde ai valori specificati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-960">Each endpoint's `RoutePattern` is evaluated until a route pattern that matches the supplied values is found.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-961">L'output risultante viene unito alle altre parti dell'URI specificate nel generatore di collegamenti e restituito.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-961">The resulting output is combined with the other URI parts supplied to the link generator and returned.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-962">I metodi forniti da <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> supportano le funzionalità di generazione di collegamenti standard per tutti i tipi di indirizzi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-962">The methods provided by <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> support standard link generation capabilities for any type of address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-963">È consigliabile usare il generatore di collegamenti tramite i metodi di estensione che eseguono le operazioni per un tipo di indirizzo specifico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-963">The most convenient way to use the link generator is through extension methods that perform operations for a specific address type.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="3658d-964">Metodo di estensione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-964">Extension Method</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-965">Descrizione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-965">Description</span></span>                                                         |
| ------------------ | ------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-966">Genera un URI con un percorso assoluto in base ai valori specificati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-966">Generates a URI with an absolute path based on the provided values.</span></span> |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetUriByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-967">Genera un URI assoluto in base ai valori specificati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-967">Generates an absolute URI based on the provided values.</span></span>             |

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-968">Prestare attenzione alle implicazioni seguenti della chiamata ai metodi <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator>:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-968">Pay attention to the following implications of calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> methods:</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-969">Usare i metodi di estensione `GetUri*` con cautela in una configurazione di app che non convalida l'intestazione `Host` delle richieste in ingresso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-969">Use `GetUri*` extension methods with caution in an app configuration that doesn't validate the `Host` header of incoming requests.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-970">Se l'intestazione `Host` delle richieste in ingresso non viene convalidata, l'input delle richieste non attendibili può essere inviato nuovamente al client negli URI di una visualizzazione o pagina.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-970">If the `Host` header of incoming requests isn't validated, untrusted request input can be sent back to the client in URIs in a view/page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-971">È consigliabile che in tutte le app di produzione il server sia configurato per la convalida dell'intestazione `Host` rispetto ai valori validi noti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-971">We recommend that all production apps configure their server to validate the `Host` header against known valid values.</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="3658d-972">Usare <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> con cautela nel middleware in associazione a `Map` o `MapWhen`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-972">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> with caution in middleware in combination with `Map` or `MapWhen`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-973">`Map*` modifica il percorso di base della richiesta in esecuzione, che ha effetto sull'output della generazione di collegamenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-973">`Map*` changes the base path of the executing request, which affects the output of link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-974">Tutte le API <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> consentono di specificare un percorso di base.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-974">All of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> APIs allow specifying a base path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-975">Specificare sempre un percorso di base vuoto per annullare l'effetto di `Map*` sulla generazione di collegamenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-975">Always specify an empty base path to undo `Map*`'s affect on link generation.</span></span>

## <a name="differences-from-earlier-versions-of-routing"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-976">Differenze rispetto alle versioni precedenti del routing</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-976">Differences from earlier versions of routing</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-977">Tra il routing di endpoint in ASP.NET Core 2.2 o versioni successive e le versioni precedenti del routing in ASP.NET Core esistono alcune differenze:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-977">A few differences exist between endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later and earlier versions of routing in ASP.NET Core:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-978">Il sistema di routing di endpoint non supporta l'estensibilità basata su <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>, inclusa l'eredità da <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-978">The endpoint routing system doesn't support <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based extensibility, including inheriting from <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-979">Il routing di endpoint non supporta [WebApiCompatShim](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.WebApiCompatShim).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-979">Endpoint routing doesn't support [WebApiCompatShim](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.WebApiCompatShim).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-980">Usare la [versione di compatibilità](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) 2.1 (`.SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_1)`) per continuare a usare lo shim per la compatibilità.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-980">Use the 2.1 [compatibility version](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) (`.SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_1)`) to continue using the compatibility shim.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-981">Il routing di endpoint ha un comportamento diverso per l'utilizzo delle maiuscole e delle minuscole degli URI generati quando si usano le route convenzionali.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-981">Endpoint Routing has different behavior for the casing of generated URIs when using conventional routes.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="3658d-982">Esaminare il modello di route predefinito seguente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-982">Consider the following default route template:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  app.UseMvc(routes =>
  {
      routes.MapRoute("default", "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
  });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="3658d-983">Si supponga di generare un collegamento a un'azione usando la route seguente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-983">Suppose you generate a link to an action using the following route:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  var link = Url.Action("ReadPost", "blog", new { id = 17, });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="3658d-984">Con il routing basato su <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>, questo codice genera un URI di `/blog/ReadPost/17`, che rispetta le maiuscole e le minuscole del valore di route specificato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-984">With <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>-based routing, this code generates a URI of `/blog/ReadPost/17`, which respects the casing of the provided route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-985">Il routing di endpoint in ASP.NET Core 2.2 o versioni successive produce `/Blog/ReadPost/17` ("Blog" viene convertita in lettere maiuscole).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-985">Endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later produces `/Blog/ReadPost/17` ("Blog" is capitalized).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-986">Il routing di endpoint offre l'interfaccia `IOutboundParameterTransformer` che può essere usata per personalizzare questo comportamento globalmente o per applicare convenzioni diverse per il mapping degli URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-986">Endpoint routing provides the `IOutboundParameterTransformer` interface that can be used to customize this behavior globally or to apply different conventions for mapping URLs.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="3658d-987">Per altre informazioni, vedere la sezione [Riferimento ai trasformatori di parametro](#parameter-transformer-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-987">For more information, see the [Parameter transformer reference](#parameter-transformer-reference) section.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-988">La generazione di collegamenti usata da MVC o Razor Pages con le route convenzionali ha un comportamento diverso quando si tenta il collegamento a un controller/azione o a una pagina non esistente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-988">Link Generation used by MVC/Razor Pages with conventional routes behaves differently when attempting to link to an controller/action or page that doesn't exist.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="3658d-989">Esaminare il modello di route predefinito seguente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-989">Consider the following default route template:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  app.UseMvc(routes =>
  {
      routes.MapRoute("default", "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
  });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="3658d-990">Si supponga di generare un collegamento a un'azione usando il modello predefinito con il codice seguente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-990">Suppose you generate a link to an action using the default template with the following:</span></span>

  ```csharp
  var link = Url.Action("ReadPost", "Blog", new { id = 17, });
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="3658d-991">Con il routing basato su `IRouter`, il risultato è sempre `/Blog/ReadPost/17`, anche se `BlogController` non è presente o non ha un metodo di azione `ReadPost`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-991">With `IRouter`-based routing, the result is always `/Blog/ReadPost/17`, even if the `BlogController` doesn't exist or doesn't have a `ReadPost` action method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-992">Come previsto, il routing di endpoint in ASP.NET Core 2.2 o versioni successive produce `/Blog/ReadPost/17` se è presente il metodo di azione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-992">As expected, endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later produces `/Blog/ReadPost/17` if the action method exists.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-993">*Tuttavia, il routing di endpoint produce una stringa vuota se l'azione non è presente.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-993">*However, endpoint routing produces an empty string if the action doesn't exist.*</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-994">Concettualmente, il routing di endpoint non presume che l'endpoint sia presente se l'azione non è presente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-994">Conceptually, endpoint routing doesn't assume that the endpoint exists if the action doesn't exist.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-995">L'*algoritmo di invalidamento dei valori di ambiente* della generazione di collegamenti ha un comportamento diverso quando viene usato con il routing di endpoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-995">The link generation *ambient value invalidation algorithm* behaves differently when used with endpoint routing.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="3658d-996">L'*invalidamento dei valori di ambiente* è l'algoritmo che decide quali valori di route della richiesta in esecuzione (valori di ambiente) possono essere usati nelle operazioni di generazione di collegamenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-996">*Ambient value invalidation* is the algorithm that decides which route values from the currently executing request (the ambient values) can be used in link generation operations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-997">Il routing convenzionale ha sempre invalidato i valori di route aggiuntivi durante il collegamento a un'azione diversa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-997">Conventional routing always invalidated extra route values when linking to a different action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-998">Prima del rilascio di ASP.NET Core 2.2, il routing degli attributi non aveva questo comportamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-998">Attribute routing didn't have this behavior prior to the release of ASP.NET Core 2.2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-999">Nelle versioni precedenti di ASP.NET Core i collegamenti a un'altra azione con gli stessi nomi di parametro di route causavano errori nella generazione dei collegamenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-999">In earlier versions of ASP.NET Core, links to another action that use the same route parameter names resulted in link generation errors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1000">In ASP.NET Core 2.2 o versioni successive entrambi i tipi di routing invalidano i valori in caso di collegamento a un'altra azione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1000">In ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later, both forms of routing invalidate values when linking to another action.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1001">Esaminare l'esempio seguente in ASP.NET Core 2.1 o versioni precedenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1001">Consider the following example in ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1002">In caso di collegamento a un'altra azione o a un'altra pagina, i valori di route possono essere riutilizzati in modi indesiderati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1002">When linking to another action (or another page), route values can be reused in undesirable ways.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1003">In */Pages/Store/Product.cshtml*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1003">In */Pages/Store/Product.cshtml*:</span></span>

  ```cshtml
  @page "{id}"
  @Url.Page("/Login")
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1004">In */Pages/Login.cshtml*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1004">In */Pages/Login.cshtml*:</span></span>

  ```cshtml
  @page "{id?}"
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1005">Se l'URI è `/Store/Product/18` in ASP.NET Core 2.1 o versioni precedenti, il collegamento generato nella pagina Store/Info da `@Url.Page("/Login")` è `/Login/18`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1005">If the URI is `/Store/Product/18` in ASP.NET Core 2.1 or earlier, the link generated on the Store/Info page by `@Url.Page("/Login")` is `/Login/18`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1006">Il valore `id` di 18 viene riutilizzato, anche se la destinazione del collegamento è una parte diversa dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1006">The `id` value of 18 is reused, even though the link destination is different part of the app entirely.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1007">Il valore di route `id` nel contesto della pagina `/Login` è probabilmente un valore di ID utente, non un valore di ID prodotto del punto vendita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1007">The `id` route value in the context of the `/Login` page is probably a user ID value, not a store product ID value.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1008">Nel routing di endpoint con ASP.NET Core 2.2 o versioni successive, il risultato è `/Login`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1008">In endpoint routing with ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later, the result is `/Login`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1009">I valori di ambiente non vengono riutilizzati quando la destinazione collegata è costituita da un'azione o una pagina diversa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1009">Ambient values aren't reused when the linked destination is a different action or page.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1010">Sintassi dei parametri di route di round trip: le barre non vengono codificate quando viene usata una sintassi del parametro catch-all con doppio asterisco (`**`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1010">Round-tripping route parameter syntax: Forward slashes aren't encoded when using a double-asterisk (`**`) catch-all parameter syntax.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1011">Durante la generazione di collegamenti, il sistema di routing codifica il valore acquisito in un parametro catch-all con doppio asterisco (`**`) (ad esempio, `{**myparametername}`) escludendo le barre.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1011">During link generation, the routing system encodes the value captured in a double-asterisk (`**`) catch-all parameter (for example, `{**myparametername}`) except the forward slashes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1012">Il parametro catch-all con doppio asterisco è supportato con il routing basato su `IRouter` in ASP.NET Core 2.2 o versioni successive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1012">The double-asterisk catch-all is supported with `IRouter`-based routing in ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1013">La sintassi del parametro catch-all con asterisco singolo nelle versioni precedenti di ASP.NET Core (`{*myparametername}`) resta supportata e le barre vengono codificate.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1013">The single asterisk catch-all parameter syntax in prior versions of ASP.NET Core (`{*myparametername}`) remains supported, and forward slashes are encoded.</span></span>

  | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1014">Route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1014">Route</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1015">Collegamento generato con</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1015">Link generated with</span></span><br>`Url.Action(new { category = "admin/products" })`&hellip; |
  | ------------------ | --------------------------------------------------------------------- |
  | `/search/{*page}`  | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1016">`/search/admin%2Fproducts` (la barra viene codificata)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1016">`/search/admin%2Fproducts` (the forward slash is encoded)</span></span>             |
  | `/search/{**page}` | `/search/admin/products`                                              |

### <a name="middleware-example"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-1017">Esempio di middleware</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1017">Middleware example</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1018">Nell'esempio seguente un middleware usa l'API <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> per creare il collegamento a un metodo di azione che elenca i prodotti del punto vendita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1018">In the following example, a middleware uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API to create link to an action method that lists store products.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1019">L'uso del generatore di collegamenti tramite l'inserimento in una classe e la chiamata a `GenerateLink` è possibile in tutte le classi di un'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1019">Using the link generator by injecting it into a class and calling `GenerateLink` is available to any class in an app.</span></span>

```csharp
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing;

public class ProductsLinkMiddleware
{
    private readonly LinkGenerator _linkGenerator;

    public ProductsLinkMiddleware(RequestDelegate next, LinkGenerator linkGenerator)
    {
        _linkGenerator = linkGenerator;
    }

    public async Task InvokeAsync(HttpContext httpContext)
    {
        var url = _linkGenerator.GetPathByAction("ListProducts", "Store");

        httpContext.Response.ContentType = "text/plain";

        await httpContext.Response.WriteAsync($"Go to {url} to see our products.");
    }
}
```

### <a name="create-routes"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-1020">Creazione di route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1020">Create routes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1021">La maggior parte delle app crea le route chiamando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> o uno dei metodi di estensione simili definiti per <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1021">Most apps create routes by calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> or one of the similar extension methods defined on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1022">Tutti i metodi di estensione <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> creano un'istanza di <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> e la aggiungono alla raccolta di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1022">Any of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> extension methods create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> and add it to the route collection.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1023"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> non accetta alcun parametro del gestore di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1023"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> doesn't accept a route handler parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1024"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> aggiunge solo le route che sono gestite da <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1024"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> only adds routes that are handled by the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1025">Per altre informazioni sul routing in MVC, vedere <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1025">To learn more about routing in MVC, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1026">L'esempio di codice seguente si riferisce a una chiamata <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> usata da una tipica definizione di route di ASP.NET Core MVC:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1026">The following code example is an example of a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> call used by a typical ASP.NET Core MVC route definition:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1027">Questo modello confronta un percorso URL ed estrae i valori di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1027">This template matches a URL path and extracts the route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1028">Ad esempio, il percorso `/Products/Details/17` genera i valori di route seguenti: `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1028">For example, the path `/Products/Details/17` generates the following route values: `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1029">I valori di route vengono determinati suddividendo il percorso URL in segmenti e confrontando ogni segmento con il nome del *parametro di route* nel modello di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1029">Route values are determined by splitting the URL path into segments and matching each segment with the *route parameter* name in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1030">I parametri di route sono denominati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1030">Route parameters are named.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1031">Parametri definiti racchiudendo il nome del parametro tra parentesi graffe `{ ... }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1031">The parameters defined by enclosing the parameter name in braces `{ ... }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1032">Il modello precedente può anche confrontare il percorso URL `/` e generare i valori `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1032">The preceding template could also match the URL path `/` and produce the values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1033">Ciò accade perché i parametri di route `{controller}` e `{action}` hanno valori predefiniti e il parametro di route `id` è facoltativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1033">This occurs because the `{controller}` and `{action}` route parameters have default values and the `id` route parameter is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1034">Un segno di uguale (`=`) seguito da un valore dopo il nome del parametro di route definisce un valore predefinito per il parametro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1034">An equals sign (`=`) followed by a value after the route parameter name defines a default value for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1035">Un punto interrogativo (`?`) dopo il nome del parametro di route definisce un parametro facoltativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1035">A question mark (`?`) after the route parameter name defines an optional parameter.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1036">I parametri di route con un valore predefinito producono *sempre* un valore di route quando la route corrisponde.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1036">Route parameters with a default value *always* produce a route value when the route matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1037">I parametri facoltativi non producono un valore di route se non è presente un segmento di percorso URL corrispondente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1037">Optional parameters don't produce a route value if there is no corresponding URL path segment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1038">Vedere la sezione [Riferimento per i modelli di route](#route-template-reference) per una descrizione completa degli scenari e della sintassi del modello di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1038">See the [Route template reference](#route-template-reference) section for a thorough description of route template scenarios and syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1039">Nell'esempio seguente la definizione del parametro di route `{id:int}` definisce un [vincolo di route](#route-constraint-reference) per il parametro di route `id`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1039">In the following example, the route parameter definition `{id:int}` defines a [route constraint](#route-constraint-reference) for the `id` route parameter:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id:int}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1040">Questo modello confronta un percorso URL come `/Products/Details/17`, ma non `/Products/Details/Apples`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1040">This template matches a URL path like `/Products/Details/17` but not `/Products/Details/Apples`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1041">I vincoli di route implementano <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> ed esaminano i valori di route per verificarli.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1041">Route constraints implement <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> and inspect route values to verify them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1042">In questo esempio il valore di route `id` deve poter essere convertito in un numero intero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1042">In this example, the route value `id` must be convertible to an integer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1043">Vedere [Riferimento per i vincoli di route](#route-constraint-reference) per una descrizione dei vincoli di route specificati dal framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1043">See [route-constraint-reference](#route-constraint-reference) for an explanation of route constraints provided by the framework.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1044">Altri overload di <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> accettano i valori per `constraints`, `dataTokens` e `defaults`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1044">Additional overloads of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> accept values for `constraints`, `dataTokens`, and `defaults`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1045">L'uso tipico di questi parametri è passare un oggetto tipizzato in modo anonimo, in cui i nomi di proprietà di tipo anonimo corrispondono ai nomi dei parametri di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1045">The typical usage of these parameters is to pass an anonymously typed object, where the property names of the anonymous type match route parameter names.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1046">Gli esempi <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> seguenti creano route equivalenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1046">The following <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> examples create equivalent routes:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller}/{action}/{id?}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Home", action = "Index" });

routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1047">La sintassi inline per definire i vincoli e i valori predefiniti può essere utile per le route semplici.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1047">The inline syntax for defining constraints and defaults can be convenient for simple routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1048">Esistono tuttavia scenari, come i token di dati, che non sono supportati dalla sintassi inline.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1048">However, there are scenarios, such as data tokens, that aren't supported by inline syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1049">L'esempio seguente illustra alcuni scenari aggiuntivi:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1049">The following example demonstrates a few additional scenarios:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "blog",
    template: "Blog/{**article}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadArticle" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1050">Il modello precedente confronta un percorso URL come `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` ed estrae i valori `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1050">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` and extracts the values `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1051">I valori di route predefiniti per `controller` e `action` vengono generati dalla route anche se sono non presenti parametri di route corrispondenti nel modello.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1051">The default route values for `controller` and `action` are produced by the route even though there are no corresponding route parameters in the template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1052">I valori predefiniti possono essere specificati nel modello di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1052">Default values can be specified in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1053">Il parametro di route `article` è definito come *catch-all* in base alla presenza di un doppio asterisco (`**`) prima del nome del parametro di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1053">The `article` route parameter is defined as a *catch-all* by the appearance of an double asterisk (`**`) before the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1054">I parametri di route catch-all acquisiscono il resto del percorso URL e possono anche corrispondere alla stringa vuota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1054">Catch-all route parameters capture the remainder of the URL path and can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1055">L'esempio seguente aggiunge i vincoli di route e i token di dati:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1055">The following example adds route constraints and data tokens:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "us_english_products",
    template: "en-US/Products/{id}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Products", action = "Details" },
    constraints: new { id = new IntRouteConstraint() },
    dataTokens: new { locale = "en-US" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1056">Il modello precedente confronta un percorso URL come `/en-US/Products/5` ed estrae i valori `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` e i token di dati `{ locale = en-US }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1056">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/en-US/Products/5` and extracts the values `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` and the data tokens `{ locale = en-US }`.</span></span>

![Token della finestra Variabili locali](routing/_static/tokens.png)

### <a name="route-class-url-generation"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-1058">Generazione di URL della classe di route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1058">Route class URL generation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1059">La classe <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> è inoltre in grado di eseguire la generazione di URL combinando un set di valori di route con il relativo modello di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1059">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class can also perform URL generation by combining a set of route values with its route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1060">Questo è logicamente il processo inverso di corrispondenza del percorso URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1060">This is logically the reverse process of matching the URL path.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1061">Per comprendere meglio la generazione di URL, si pensi a quale URL si vuole generare e al modo in cui un modello di route deve corrispondere a tale URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1061">To better understand URL generation, imagine what URL you want to generate and then think about how a route template would match that URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1062">Quali valori devono essere prodotti?</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1062">What values would be produced?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1063">Questo equivale approssimativamente al funzionamento della generazione di URL nella classe <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1063">This is the rough equivalent of how URL generation works in the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1064">L'esempio seguente usa una route predefinita di ASP.NET Core MVC generale:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1064">The following example uses a general ASP.NET Core MVC default route:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1065">Con i valori di route `{ controller = Products, action = List }`, viene generato l'URL `/Products/List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1065">With the route values `{ controller = Products, action = List }`, the URL `/Products/List` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1066">I valori di route vengono sostituiti dai parametri di route corrispondenti per formare il percorso URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1066">The route values are substituted for the corresponding route parameters to form the URL path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1067">Poiché `id` è un parametro di route facoltativo, l'URL è stato generato senza un valore per `id`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1067">Since `id` is an optional route parameter, the URL is successfully generated without a value for `id`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1068">Con i valori di route `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`, viene generato l'URL `/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1068">With the route values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`, the URL `/` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1069">Poiché i valori di route specificati corrispondono ai valori predefiniti, i segmenti corrispondenti ai valori predefiniti possono essere omessi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1069">The provided route values match the default values, and the segments corresponding to the default values are safely omitted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1070">Per entrambi gli URL generati viene eseguito il round trip con la definizione di route seguente (`/Home/Index` e `/`) e vengono prodotti gli stessi valori di route usati per generare l'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1070">Both URLs generated round-trip with the following route definition (`/Home/Index` and `/`) produce the same route values that were used to generate the URL.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1071">Un'app che usa ASP.NET Core MVC deve usare <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> per generare gli URL invece di eseguire la chiamata direttamente nel routing.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1071">An app using ASP.NET Core MVC should use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> to generate URLs instead of calling into routing directly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1072">Per altre informazioni sulla generazione di URL, vedere la sezione [Riferimento per la generazione di URL](#url-generation-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1072">For more information on URL generation, see the [Url generation reference](#url-generation-reference) section.</span></span>

## <a name="use-routing-middleware"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-1073">Usare il middleware di routing</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1073">Use Routing Middleware</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1074">Fare riferimento al [metapacchetto Microsoft.AspNetCore.App](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) nel file di progetto dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1074">Reference the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App metapackage](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) in the app's project file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1075">Aggiungere il routing al contenitore del servizio in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1075">Add routing to the service container in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_ConfigureServices&highlight=3)]

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1076">Le route devono essere configurate nel metodo `Startup.Configure`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1076">Routes must be configured in the `Startup.Configure` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1077">L'app di esempio usa le API seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1077">The sample app uses the following APIs:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1078"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> &ndash; corrisponde solo alle richieste HTTP GET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1078"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> &ndash; Matches only HTTP GET requests.</span></span>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*>

| <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1080">URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1080">URI</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1081">Risposta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1081">Response</span></span>                                          |

| `/package/track/`      | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1088">La richiesta non viene eseguita, nessuna corrispondenza.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1088">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |
| `GET /hello/Joe`       | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1089">Hi, Joe!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1089">Hi, Joe!</span></span>                                          |
| `POST /hello/Joe`      | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1090">La richiesta non viene eseguita, corrispondenza solo con HTTP GET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1090">The request falls through, matches HTTP GET only.</span></span> |
| `GET /hello/Joe/Smith` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1091">La richiesta non viene eseguita, nessuna corrispondenza.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1091">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1092">Il framework offre un set di metodi di estensione per la creazione di route (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1092">The framework provides a set of extension methods for creating routes (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePut*>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1093">I metodi `Map[Verb]` usano i vincoli per limitare la route al verbo HTTP nel nome del metodo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1093">The `Map[Verb]` methods use constraints to limit the route to the HTTP Verb in the method name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1094">Vedere ad esempio <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> e <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1094">For example, see <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span></span>

## <a name="route-template-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-1095">Riferimento per il modello di route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1095">Route template reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1096">I token all'interno di parentesi graffe (`{ ... }`) definiscono i *parametri di route* che vengono associati se esiste una corrispondenza per la route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1096">Tokens within curly braces (`{ ... }`) define *route parameters* that are bound if the route is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1097">È possibile definire più parametri di route in un segmento di route, ma devono essere separati da un valore letterale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1097">You can define more than one route parameter in a route segment, but they must be separated by a literal value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1098">Ad esempio, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` non è una route valida perché non è presente un valore letterale tra `{controller}` e `{action}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1098">For example, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` isn't a valid route, since there's no literal value between `{controller}` and `{action}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1099">Questi parametri di route devono avere un nome e possono avere attributi aggiuntivi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1099">These route parameters must have a name and may have additional attributes specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1100">Il testo letterale diverso dai parametri di route, ad esempio `{id}`, e il separatore di percorso `/` devono corrispondere al testo nell'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1100">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1101">La corrispondenza del testo non fa distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole e si basa sulla rappresentazione decodificata del percorso degli URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1101">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URLs path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1102">Per verificare la corrispondenza di un delimitatore letterale dei parametri di route (`{` o `}`), eseguire l'escape del delimitatore ripetendo il carattere (`{{` o `}}`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1102">To match a literal route parameter delimiter (`{` or `}`), escape the delimiter by repeating the character (`{{` or `}}`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1103">I modelli di URL che tentano di acquisire un nome file con un'estensione facoltativa hanno considerazioni aggiuntive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1103">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1104">Considerare ad esempio il modello `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1104">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1105">Se esistono i valori per `filename` e `ext`, vengono popolati entrambi i valori.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1105">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1106">Se esiste solo un valore per `filename` nell'URL, la route corrisponde perché il punto finale (`.`) è facoltativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1106">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing period (`.`) is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1107">Gli URL seguenti corrispondono a questa route:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1107">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1108">È possibile usare un asterisco (`*`) o un doppio asterisco (`**`) come prefisso per un parametro di route da associare alla parte rimanente dell'URI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1108">You can use an asterisk (`*`) or double asterisk (`**`) as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1109">Si tratta di parametri chiamati parametri *catch-all*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1109">These are called a *catch-all* parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1110">Ad esempio, `blog/{**slug}` corrisponde a qualsiasi URI che inizia con `/blog` seguito da qualsiasi valore, che viene assegnato al valore di route `slug`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1110">For example, `blog/{**slug}` matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it, which is assigned to the `slug` route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1111">I parametri catch-all possono anche corrispondere alla stringa vuota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1111">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1112">Il parametro catch-all esegue l'escape dei caratteri appropriati, incluso il separatore di percorso (`/`), quando la route viene usata per generare un URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1112">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator (`/`) characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1113">Ad esempio, la route `foo/{*path}` con i valori di route `{ path = "my/path" }` genera `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1113">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1114">Si noti la barra di escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1114">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1115">Per eseguire il round trip dei caratteri di separatore di percorso, usare il prefisso del parametro di route `**`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1115">To round-trip path separator characters, use the `**` route parameter prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1116">La route `foo/{**path}` con `{ path = "my/path" }` genera `foo/my/path`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1116">The route `foo/{**path}` with `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my/path`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1117">I parametri di route possono avere *valori predefiniti*, definiti specificando il valore predefinito dopo il nome del parametro, separato da un segno di uguale (`=`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1117">Route parameters may have *default values* designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1118">Ad esempio, `{controller=Home}` definisce `Home` come valore predefinito per `controller`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1118">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1119">Il valore predefinito viene usato se nell'URL non è presente alcun valore per il parametro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1119">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1120">I parametri di route vengono resi facoltativi aggiungendo un punto interrogativo (`?`) alla fine del nome del parametro, come in `id?`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1120">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name, as in `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1121">La differenza tra parametri facoltativi e parametri di route predefiniti è che un parametro di route con un valore predefinito produce sempre un valore, mentre un parametro facoltativo ha un valore solo se ne viene specificato uno dall'URL della richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1121">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is that a route parameter with a default value always produces a value&mdash;an optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1122">I parametri di route possono presentare dei vincoli che devono corrispondere al valore di route associato dall'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1122">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1123">Aggiungendo due punti (`:`) e il nome del vincolo dopo il nome del parametro di route, si specifica un *vincolo inline* per un parametro di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1123">Adding a colon (`:`) and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an *inline constraint* on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1124">Se il vincolo richiede argomenti, vengono racchiusi tra parentesi (`(...)`) dopo il nome del vincolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1124">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses (`(...)`) after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1125">È possibile specificare più vincoli inline aggiungendo di nuovo i due punti (`:`) e il nome del vincolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1125">Multiple inline constraints can be specified by appending another colon (`:`) and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1126">Il nome del vincolo e gli argomenti vengono passati al servizio <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> per creare un'istanza di <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> da usare nell'elaborazione dell'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1126">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1127">Il modello di route `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifica ad esempio un vincolo `minlength` con l'argomento `10`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1127">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1128">Per altre informazioni sui vincoli di route e per un elenco dei vincoli specificati dal framework, vedere la sezione [Riferimento per i vincoli di route](#route-constraint-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1128">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1129">I parametri di route possono avere anche trasformatori di parametro che trasformano un valore di parametro durante la generazione dei collegamenti e l'abbinamento delle azioni e delle pagine agli URI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1129">Route parameters may also have parameter transformers, which transform a parameter's value when generating links and matching actions and pages to URLs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1130">Come i vincoli, i trasformatori di parametro possono essere aggiunti inline a un parametro di route inserendo due punti (`:`) e il nome del trasformatore dopo il nome del parametro di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1130">Like constraints, parameter transformers can be added inline to a route parameter by adding a colon (`:`) and transformer name after the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1131">Ad esempio, il modello di route `blog/{article:slugify}` specifica un trasformatore `slugify`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1131">For example, the route template `blog/{article:slugify}` specifies a `slugify` transformer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1132">Per altre informazioni sui trasformatori di parametro, vedere la sezione [Riferimento ai trasformatori di parametro](#parameter-transformer-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1132">For more information on parameter transformers, see the [Parameter transformer reference](#parameter-transformer-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1133">La tabella seguente illustra i modelli di route di esempio e il relativo comportamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1133">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1134">Modello di route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1134">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1135">URI corrispondente di esempio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1135">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1136">L'URI della richiesta&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1136">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1137">Verifica la corrispondenza solo del singolo percorso `/hello`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1137">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1138">Verifica la corrispondenza e imposta `Page` su `Home`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1138">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1139">Verifica la corrispondenza e imposta `Page` su `Contact`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1139">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1140">Esegue il mapping al controller `Products` e all'azione `List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1140">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1141">Esegue il mapping al controller `Products` e all'azione `Details` (`id` impostato su 123).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1141">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action (`id` set to 123).</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1142">Esegue il mapping al controller `Home` e al metodo `Index` (`id` viene ignorato).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1142">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method (`id` is ignored).</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1143">L'uso di un modello è in genere l'approccio più semplice al routing.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1143">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1144">I vincoli e le impostazioni predefinite possono essere specificati anche all'esterno del modello di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1144">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1145">Abilitare la [registrazione](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) per verificare in che modo le implementazioni del routing predefinite, ad esempio <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, corrispondono alle richieste.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1145">Enable [Logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) to see how the built-in routing implementations, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, match requests.</span></span>

## <a name="reserved-routing-names"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-1146">Nomi riservati di routing</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1146">Reserved routing names</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1147">Le parole chiave seguenti sono nomi riservati e non possono essere usate come nomi o parametri di route:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1147">The following keywords are reserved names and can't be used as route names or parameters:</span></span>

* `action`
* `area`
* `controller`
* `handler`
* `page`

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-1148">Riferimento per i vincoli di route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1148">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1149">I vincoli di route vengono eseguiti quando si verifica una corrispondenza nell'URL in ingresso e il percorso URL viene suddiviso in valori di route in formato token.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1149">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1150">I vincoli di route in genere controllano il valore di route associato usando il modello di route e stabiliscono con una decisione Sì/No se il valore è accettabile o meno.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1150">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a yes/no decision about whether or not the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1151">Alcuni vincoli di route usano i dati all'esterno del valore di route per stabilire se la richiesta può essere instradata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1151">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1152">Ad esempio, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> può accettare o rifiutare una richiesta in base al relativo verbo HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1152">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1153">I vincoli vengono usati nelle richieste del routing e nella generazione di collegamenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1153">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1154">Non usare i vincoli per la **convalida dell'input**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1154">Don't use constraints for **input validation**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1155">Se vengono usati vincoli per la **convalida dell'input**, un input non valido causa la visualizzazione di un errore di tipo *404 (Non trovato)* invece di un errore di tipo *400 - Richiesta non valida* con un messaggio di errore appropriato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1155">If constraints are used for **input validation**, invalid input results in a *404 - Not Found* response instead of a *400 - Bad Request* with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1156">I vincoli di route vengono usati per evitare **ambiguità** tra route simili, non per convalidare gli input per una route specifica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1156">Route constraints are used to **disambiguate** similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1157">La tabella seguente illustra i vincoli di route di esempio e il relativo comportamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1157">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1158">vincolo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1158">constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1159">Esempio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1159">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1160">Esempi di corrispondenza</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1160">Example Matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1161">Note</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1161">Notes</span></span> |
| ---------- | ------- | --------------- | ----- |
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1162">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1162">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1163">Corrisponde a qualsiasi numero intero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1163">Matches any integer.</span></span> |
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1164">`true`, `FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1164">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1165">Corrisponde `true` o ' false.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1165">Matches `true` or \`false.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1166">Senza distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1166">Case-insensitive.</span></span> |
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1167">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1167">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1168">Corrisponde a un valore `DateTime` valido nella lingua inglese.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1168">Matches a valid `DateTime` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1169">Vedere l'avviso precedente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1169">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `decimal` | `{price:decimal}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1170">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1170">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1171">Corrisponde a un valore `decimal` valido nella lingua inglese.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1171">Matches a valid `decimal` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1172">Vedere l'avviso precedente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1172">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `double` | `{weight:double}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1173">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1173">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1174">Corrisponde a un valore `double` valido nella lingua inglese.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1174">Matches a valid `double` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1175">Vedere l'avviso precedente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1175">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `float` | `{weight:float}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1176">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1176">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1177">Corrisponde a un valore `float` valido nella lingua inglese.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1177">Matches a valid `float` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1178">Vedere l'avviso precedente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1178">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `guid` | `{id:guid}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1179">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1179">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1180">Corrisponde a un valore di `Guid` valido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1180">Matches a valid `Guid` value.</span></span> |
| `long` | `{ticks:long}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1181">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1181">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1182">Corrisponde a un valore di `long` valido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1182">Matches a valid `long` value.</span></span> |
| `minlength(value)` | `{username:minlength(4)}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1183">La stringa deve contenere almeno 4 caratteri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1183">String must be at least 4 characters.</span></span> |
| `maxlength(value)` | `{filename:maxlength(8)}` | `MyFile` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1184">La stringa ha un massimo di 8 caratteri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1184">String has maximum of 8 characters.</span></span> |
| `length(length)` | `{filename:length(12)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1185">La lunghezza della stringa deve essere uguale a 12 caratteri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1185">String must be exactly 12 characters long.</span></span> |
| `length(min,max)` | `{filename:length(8,16)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1186">La stringa deve essere almeno 8 e può contenere un massimo di 16 caratteri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1186">String must be at least 8 and has maximum of 16 characters.</span></span> |
| `min(value)` | `{age:min(18)}` | `19` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1187">Il valore intero deve essere almeno 18.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1187">Integer value must be at least 18.</span></span> |
| `max(value)` | `{age:max(120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1188">Valore intero massimo di 120.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1188">Integer value maximum of 120.</span></span> |
| `range(min,max)` | `{age:range(18,120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1189">Il valore intero deve essere almeno 18 e un massimo di 120.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1189">Integer value must be at least 18 and maximum of 120.</span></span> |
| `alpha` | `{name:alpha}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1190">La stringa deve essere costituita da uno o più caratteri alfabetici `a`-`z`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1190">String must consist of one or more alphabetical characters `a`-`z`.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1191">Senza distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1191">Case-insensitive.</span></span> |
| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1192">La stringa deve corrispondere all'espressione regolare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1192">String must match the regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1193">Vedere suggerimenti sulla definizione di un'espressione regolare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1193">See tips about defining a regular expression.</span></span> |
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1194">Utilizzato per imporre che un valore non di parametro sia presente durante la generazione dell'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1194">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation.</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1195">Più vincoli delimitati da punti possono essere applicati a un singolo parametro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1195">Multiple, colon-delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1196">Ad esempio il vincolo seguente limita un parametro a un valore intero maggiore o uguale a 1:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1196">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
