> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1429">La sintassi inline per definire i vincoli e i valori predefiniti può essere utile per le route semplici.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1429">The inline syntax for defining constraints and defaults can be convenient for simple routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1430">Esistono tuttavia scenari, come i token di dati, che non sono supportati dalla sintassi inline.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1430">However, there are scenarios, such as data tokens, that aren't supported by inline syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1431">L'esempio seguente illustra alcuni scenari aggiuntivi:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1431">The following example demonstrates a few additional scenarios:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "blog",
    template: "Blog/{*article}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadArticle" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1432">Il modello precedente confronta un percorso URL come `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` ed estrae i valori `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1432">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` and extracts the values `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1433">I valori di route predefiniti per `controller` e `action` vengono generati dalla route anche se sono non presenti parametri di route corrispondenti nel modello.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1433">The default route values for `controller` and `action` are produced by the route even though there are no corresponding route parameters in the template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1434">I valori predefiniti possono essere specificati nel modello di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1434">Default values can be specified in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1435">Il parametro di route `article` è definito come *catch-all* in base alla presenza di un asterisco (`*`) prima del nome del parametro di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1435">The `article` route parameter is defined as a *catch-all* by the appearance of an asterisk (`*`) before the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1436">I parametri di route catch-all acquisiscono il resto del percorso URL e possono anche corrispondere alla stringa vuota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1436">Catch-all route parameters capture the remainder of the URL path and can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1437">L'esempio seguente aggiunge i vincoli di route e i token di dati:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1437">The following example adds route constraints and data tokens:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "us_english_products",
    template: "en-US/Products/{id}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Products", action = "Details" },
    constraints: new { id = new IntRouteConstraint() },
    dataTokens: new { locale = "en-US" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1438">Il modello precedente confronta un percorso URL come `/en-US/Products/5` ed estrae i valori `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` e i token di dati `{ locale = en-US }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1438">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/en-US/Products/5` and extracts the values `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` and the data tokens `{ locale = en-US }`.</span></span>

![Token della finestra Variabili locali](routing/_static/tokens.png)

### <a name="route-class-url-generation"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-1440">Generazione di URL della classe di route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1440">Route class URL generation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1441">La classe <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> è inoltre in grado di eseguire la generazione di URL combinando un set di valori di route con il relativo modello di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1441">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class can also perform URL generation by combining a set of route values with its route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1442">Questo è logicamente il processo inverso di corrispondenza del percorso URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1442">This is logically the reverse process of matching the URL path.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1443">Per comprendere meglio la generazione di URL, si pensi a quale URL si vuole generare e al modo in cui un modello di route deve corrispondere a tale URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1443">To better understand URL generation, imagine what URL you want to generate and then think about how a route template would match that URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1444">Quali valori devono essere prodotti?</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1444">What values would be produced?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1445">Questo equivale approssimativamente al funzionamento della generazione di URL nella classe <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1445">This is the rough equivalent of how URL generation works in the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1446">L'esempio seguente usa una route predefinita di ASP.NET Core MVC generale:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1446">The following example uses a general ASP.NET Core MVC default route:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1447">Con i valori di route `{ controller = Products, action = List }`, viene generato l'URL `/Products/List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1447">With the route values `{ controller = Products, action = List }`, the URL `/Products/List` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1448">I valori di route vengono sostituiti dai parametri di route corrispondenti per formare il percorso URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1448">The route values are substituted for the corresponding route parameters to form the URL path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1449">Poiché `id` è un parametro di route facoltativo, l'URL è stato generato senza un valore per `id`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1449">Since `id` is an optional route parameter, the URL is successfully generated without a value for `id`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1450">Con i valori di route `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`, viene generato l'URL `/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1450">With the route values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`, the URL `/` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1451">Poiché i valori di route specificati corrispondono ai valori predefiniti, i segmenti corrispondenti ai valori predefiniti possono essere omessi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1451">The provided route values match the default values, and the segments corresponding to the default values are safely omitted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1452">Per entrambi gli URL generati viene eseguito il round trip con la definizione di route seguente (`/Home/Index` e `/`) e vengono prodotti gli stessi valori di route usati per generare l'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1452">Both URLs generated round-trip with the following route definition (`/Home/Index` and `/`) produce the same route values that were used to generate the URL.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1453">Un'app che usa ASP.NET Core MVC deve usare <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> per generare gli URL invece di eseguire la chiamata direttamente nel routing.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1453">An app using ASP.NET Core MVC should use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> to generate URLs instead of calling into routing directly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1454">Per altre informazioni sulla generazione di URL, vedere la sezione [Riferimento per la generazione di URL](#url-generation-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1454">For more information on URL generation, see the [Url generation reference](#url-generation-reference) section.</span></span>

## <a name="use-routing-middleware"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-1455">USA middleware di routing</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1455">Use routing middleware</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1456">Fare riferimento al [metapacchetto Microsoft.AspNetCore.App](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) nel file di progetto dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1456">Reference the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App metapackage](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) in the app's project file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1457">Aggiungere il routing al contenitore del servizio in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1457">Add routing to the service container in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_ConfigureServices&highlight=3)]

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1458">Le route devono essere configurate nel metodo `Startup.Configure`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1458">Routes must be configured in the `Startup.Configure` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1459">L'app di esempio usa le API seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1459">The sample app uses the following APIs:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>
* <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1460"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> &ndash; corrisponde solo alle richieste HTTP GET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1460"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> &ndash; Matches only HTTP GET requests.</span></span>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_RouteHandler)]

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1461">Nella tabella seguente sono elencate le risposte con gli URI specificati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1461">The following table shows the responses with the given URIs.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1462">URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1462">URI</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1463">Risposta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1463">Response</span></span>                                          |
| ---------------------- | ------------------------------------------------- |
| `/package/create/3`    | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1464">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1464">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1465">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1465">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3`    | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1466">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1466">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1467">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1467">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3/`   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1468">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1468">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1469">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1469">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/`      | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1470">La richiesta non viene eseguita, nessuna corrispondenza.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1470">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |
| `GET /hello/Joe`       | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1471">Hi, Joe!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1471">Hi, Joe!</span></span>                                          |
| `POST /hello/Joe`      | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1472">La richiesta non viene eseguita, corrispondenza solo con HTTP GET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1472">The request falls through, matches HTTP GET only.</span></span> |
| `GET /hello/Joe/Smith` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1473">La richiesta non viene eseguita, nessuna corrispondenza.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1473">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1474">Se si sta configurando una singola route, chiamare <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*> passando un'istanza di `IRouter`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1474">If you're configuring a single route, call <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*> passing in an `IRouter` instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1475">Non è necessario usare <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1475">You won't need to use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1476">Il framework offre un set di metodi di estensione per la creazione di route (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1476">The framework provides a set of extension methods for creating routes (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareVerb*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1477">Alcuni dei metodi elencati, ad esempio <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, richiedono <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1477">Some of listed methods, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, require a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1478"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate> viene usato come *gestore di route* quando la route corrisponde.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1478">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate> is used as the *route handler* when the route matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1479">Altri metodi di questa famiglia consentono di configurare una pipeline middleware che verrà usata come gestore di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1479">Other methods in this family allow configuring a middleware pipeline for use as the route handler.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1480">Se il metodo `Map*` non accetta un gestore, ad esempio <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>, il metodo usa <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1480">If the `Map*` method doesn't accept a handler, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>, it uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1481">I metodi `Map[Verb]` usano i vincoli per limitare la route al verbo HTTP nel nome del metodo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1481">The `Map[Verb]` methods use constraints to limit the route to the HTTP Verb in the method name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1482">Vedere ad esempio <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> e <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1482">For example, see <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span></span>

## <a name="route-template-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-1483">Riferimento per il modello di route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1483">Route template reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1484">I token all'interno di parentesi graffe (`{ ... }`) definiscono i *parametri di route* che vengono associati se esiste una corrispondenza per la route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1484">Tokens within curly braces (`{ ... }`) define *route parameters* that are bound if the route is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1485">È possibile definire più parametri di route in un segmento di route, ma devono essere separati da un valore letterale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1485">You can define more than one route parameter in a route segment, but they must be separated by a literal value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1486">Ad esempio, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` non è una route valida perché non è presente un valore letterale tra `{controller}` e `{action}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1486">For example, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` isn't a valid route, since there's no literal value between `{controller}` and `{action}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1487">Questi parametri di route devono avere un nome e possono avere attributi aggiuntivi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1487">These route parameters must have a name and may have additional attributes specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1488">Il testo letterale diverso dai parametri di route, ad esempio `{id}`, e il separatore di percorso `/` devono corrispondere al testo nell'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1488">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1489">La corrispondenza del testo non fa distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole e si basa sulla rappresentazione decodificata del percorso degli URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1489">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URLs path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1490">Per verificare la corrispondenza di un delimitatore letterale dei parametri di route (`{` o `}`), eseguire l'escape del delimitatore ripetendo il carattere (`{{` o `}}`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1490">To match a literal route parameter delimiter (`{` or `}`), escape the delimiter by repeating the character (`{{` or `}}`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1491">I modelli di URL che tentano di acquisire un nome file con un'estensione facoltativa hanno considerazioni aggiuntive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1491">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1492">Considerare ad esempio il modello `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1492">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1493">Se esistono i valori per `filename` e `ext`, vengono popolati entrambi i valori.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1493">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1494">Se esiste solo un valore per `filename` nell'URL, la route corrisponde perché il punto finale (`.`) è facoltativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1494">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing period (`.`) is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1495">Gli URL seguenti corrispondono a questa route:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1495">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1496">È possibile usare l'asterisco (`*`) come prefisso per un parametro di route da associare alla parte rimanente dell'URI,</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1496">You can use the asterisk (`*`) as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1497">ovvero un parametro *catch-all*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1497">This is called a *catch-all* parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1498">Ad esempio, `blog/{*slug}` corrisponde a qualsiasi URI che inizia con `/blog` seguito da qualsiasi valore, che viene assegnato al valore di route `slug`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1498">For example, `blog/{*slug}` matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it, which is assigned to the `slug` route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1499">I parametri catch-all possono anche corrispondere alla stringa vuota.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1499">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1500">Il parametro catch-all esegue l'escape dei caratteri appropriati, incluso il separatore di percorso (`/`), quando la route viene usata per generare un URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1500">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator (`/`) characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1501">Ad esempio, la route `foo/{*path}` con i valori di route `{ path = "my/path" }` genera `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1501">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1502">Si noti la barra di escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1502">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1503">I parametri di route possono avere *valori predefiniti*, definiti specificando il valore predefinito dopo il nome del parametro, separato da un segno di uguale (`=`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1503">Route parameters may have *default values* designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1504">Ad esempio, `{controller=Home}` definisce `Home` come valore predefinito per `controller`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1504">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1505">Il valore predefinito viene usato se nell'URL non è presente alcun valore per il parametro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1505">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1506">I parametri di route vengono resi facoltativi aggiungendo un punto interrogativo (`?`) alla fine del nome del parametro, come in `id?`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1506">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name, as in `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1507">La differenza tra parametri facoltativi e parametri di route predefiniti è che un parametro di route con un valore predefinito produce sempre un valore, mentre un parametro facoltativo ha un valore solo se ne viene specificato uno dall'URL della richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1507">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is that a route parameter with a default value always produces a value&mdash;an optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1508">I parametri di route possono presentare dei vincoli che devono corrispondere al valore di route associato dall'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1508">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1509">Aggiungendo due punti (`:`) e il nome del vincolo dopo il nome del parametro di route, si specifica un *vincolo inline* per un parametro di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1509">Adding a colon (`:`) and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an *inline constraint* on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1510">Se il vincolo richiede argomenti, vengono racchiusi tra parentesi (`(...)`) dopo il nome del vincolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1510">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses (`(...)`) after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1511">È possibile specificare più vincoli inline aggiungendo di nuovo i due punti (`:`) e il nome del vincolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1511">Multiple inline constraints can be specified by appending another colon (`:`) and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1512">Il nome del vincolo e gli argomenti vengono passati al servizio <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> per creare un'istanza di <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> da usare nell'elaborazione dell'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1512">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1513">Il modello di route `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifica ad esempio un vincolo `minlength` con l'argomento `10`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1513">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1514">Per altre informazioni sui vincoli di route e per un elenco dei vincoli specificati dal framework, vedere la sezione [Riferimento per i vincoli di route](#route-constraint-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1514">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1515">La tabella seguente illustra i modelli di route di esempio e il relativo comportamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1515">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1516">Modello di route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1516">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1517">URI corrispondente di esempio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1517">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1518">L'URI della richiesta&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1518">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1519">Verifica la corrispondenza solo del singolo percorso `/hello`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1519">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1520">Verifica la corrispondenza e imposta `Page` su `Home`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1520">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1521">Verifica la corrispondenza e imposta `Page` su `Contact`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1521">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1522">Esegue il mapping al controller `Products` e all'azione `List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1522">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1523">Esegue il mapping al controller `Products` e all'azione `Details` (`id` impostato su 123).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1523">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action (`id` set to 123).</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1524">Esegue il mapping al controller `Home` e al metodo `Index` (`id` viene ignorato).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1524">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method (`id` is ignored).</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1525">L'uso di un modello è in genere l'approccio più semplice al routing.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1525">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1526">I vincoli e le impostazioni predefinite possono essere specificati anche all'esterno del modello di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1526">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1527">Abilitare la [registrazione](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) per verificare in che modo le implementazioni del routing predefinite, ad esempio <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, corrispondono alle richieste.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1527">Enable [Logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) to see how the built-in routing implementations, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, match requests.</span></span>

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-1528">Riferimento per i vincoli di route</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1528">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1529">I vincoli di route vengono eseguiti quando si verifica una corrispondenza nell'URL in ingresso e il percorso URL viene suddiviso in valori di route in formato token.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1529">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1530">I vincoli di route in genere controllano il valore di route associato usando il modello di route e stabiliscono con una decisione Sì/No se il valore è accettabile o meno.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1530">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a yes/no decision about whether or not the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1531">Alcuni vincoli di route usano i dati all'esterno del valore di route per stabilire se la richiesta può essere instradata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1531">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1532">Ad esempio, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> può accettare o rifiutare una richiesta in base al relativo verbo HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1532">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1533">I vincoli vengono usati nelle richieste del routing e nella generazione di collegamenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1533">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1534">Non usare i vincoli per la **convalida dell'input**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1534">Don't use constraints for **input validation**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1535">Se vengono usati vincoli per la **convalida dell'input**, un input non valido causa la visualizzazione di un errore di tipo *404 (Non trovato)* invece di un errore di tipo *400 - Richiesta non valida* con un messaggio di errore appropriato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1535">If constraints are used for **input validation**, invalid input results in a *404 - Not Found* response instead of a *400 - Bad Request* with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1536">I vincoli di route vengono usati per evitare **ambiguità** tra route simili, non per convalidare gli input per una route specifica.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1536">Route constraints are used to **disambiguate** similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1537">La tabella seguente illustra i vincoli di route di esempio e il relativo comportamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1537">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1538">vincolo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1538">constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1539">Esempio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1539">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1540">Esempi di corrispondenza</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1540">Example Matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1541">Note</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1541">Notes</span></span> |
| ---------- | ------- | --------------- | ----- |
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1542">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1542">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1543">Corrisponde a qualsiasi numero intero</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1543">Matches any integer</span></span> |
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1544">`true`, `FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1544">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1545">Corrisponde a `true` o `false` (senza distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1545">Matches `true` or `false` (case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1546">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1546">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1547">Corrisponde a un valore `DateTime` valido nella lingua inglese.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1547">Matches a valid `DateTime` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1548">Vedere l'avviso precedente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1548">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `decimal` | `{price:decimal}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1549">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1549">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1550">Corrisponde a un valore `decimal` valido nella lingua inglese.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1550">Matches a valid `decimal` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1551">Vedere l'avviso precedente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1551">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `double` | `{weight:double}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1552">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1552">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1553">Corrisponde a un valore `double` valido nella lingua inglese.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1553">Matches a valid `double` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1554">Vedere l'avviso precedente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1554">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `float` | `{weight:float}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1555">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1555">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1556">Corrisponde a un valore `float` valido nella lingua inglese.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1556">Matches a valid `float` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1557">Vedere l'avviso precedente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1557">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `guid` | `{id:guid}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1558">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1558">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1559">Corrisponde a un valore `Guid` valido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1559">Matches a valid `Guid` value</span></span> |
| `long` | `{ticks:long}` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1560">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1560">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1561">Corrisponde a un valore `long` valido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1561">Matches a valid `long` value</span></span> |
| `minlength(value)` | `{username:minlength(4)}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1562">La stringa deve contenere almeno 4 caratteri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1562">String must be at least 4 characters</span></span> |
| `maxlength(value)` | `{filename:maxlength(8)}` | `Richard` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1563">La stringa non deve contenere più di 8 caratteri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1563">String must be no more than 8 characters</span></span> |
| `length(length)` | `{filename:length(12)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1564">La stringa deve contenere esattamente 12 caratteri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1564">String must be exactly 12 characters long</span></span> |
| `length(min,max)` | `{filename:length(8,16)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1565">La stringa deve contenere almeno 8 e non più di 16 caratteri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1565">String must be at least 8 and no more than 16 characters long</span></span> |
| `min(value)` | `{age:min(18)}` | `19` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1566">Il valore intero deve essere almeno 18</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1566">Integer value must be at least 18</span></span> |
| `max(value)` | `{age:max(120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1567">Il valore intero non deve essere superiore a 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1567">Integer value must be no more than 120</span></span> |
| `range(min,max)` | `{age:range(18,120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1568">Il valore intero deve essere almeno 18 ma non più di 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1568">Integer value must be at least 18 but no more than 120</span></span> |
| `alpha` | `{name:alpha}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1569">La stringa deve essere costituita da uno o più caratteri alfabetici (`a`-`z`, senza distinzione tra maiuscole e minuscole)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1569">String must consist of one or more alphabetical characters (`a`-`z`, case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1570">La stringa deve corrispondere all'espressione regolare (vedere i suggerimenti per la definizione di un'espressione regolare)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1570">String must match the regular expression (see tips about defining a regular expression)</span></span> |
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1571">Usato per imporre che un valore diverso da un parametro sia presente durante la generazione dell'URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1571">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1572">Più vincoli delimitati da punti possono essere applicati a un singolo parametro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1572">Multiple, colon-delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1573">Ad esempio il vincolo seguente limita un parametro a un valore intero maggiore o uguale a 1:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1573">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1574">I vincoli di route che verificano l'URL e vengono convertiti in un tipo CLR, ad esempio `int` o `DateTime`, usano sempre le impostazioni cultura inglese non dipendenti da paese/area geografica,</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1574">Route constraints that verify the URL and are converted to a CLR type (such as `int` or `DateTime`) always use the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1575">presupponendo che l'URL sia non localizzabile.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1575">These constraints assume that the URL is non-localizable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1576">I vincoli di route specificati dal framework non modificano i valori archiviati nei valori di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1576">The framework-provided route constraints don't modify the values stored in route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1577">Tutti i valori di route analizzati dall'URL vengono archiviati come stringhe.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1577">All route values parsed from the URL are stored as strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1578">Ad esempio, il vincolo `float` prova a convertire il valore di route in un valore float, ma il valore convertito viene usato solo per verificare che può essere convertito in un valore float.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1578">For example, the `float` constraint attempts to convert the route value to a float, but the converted value is used only to verify it can be converted to a float.</span></span>

## <a name="regular-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-1579">Espressioni regolari</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1579">Regular expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1580">Il framework di ASP.NET Core aggiunge `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` al costruttore di espressioni regolari.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1580">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1581">Per una descrizione di questi membri, vedere <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1581">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1582">Le espressioni regolari usano delimitatori e token simili a quelli usati dal routing e dal linguaggio C#.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1582">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by Routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1583">Per i token di espressione è necessario aggiungere caratteri di escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1583">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1584">Per usare l'espressione regolare `^\d`\\`-\d`\`-\d`\`$` nel routing, l'espressione deve includere i caratteri `\` (barra rovesciata singola) specificati nella stringa come caratteri `\\` (barra rovesciata doppia) nel file di origine C# per eseguire l'escape del carattere di escape della stringa `\`, a meno che non si usino [valori letterali di stringa verbatim](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1584">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in routing, the expression must have the `\` (single backslash) characters provided in the string as `\\` (double backslash) characters in the C# source file in order to escape the `\` string escape character (unless using [verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1585">Per eseguire l'escape dii caratteri delimitatori dei parametri di routing (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), raddoppiare i caratteri nell'espressione (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1585">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), double the characters in the expression (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1586">La tabella seguente mostra un'espressione regolare e la versione dopo l'escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1586">The following table shows a regular expression and the escaped version.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1587">Espressione regolare</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1587">Regular Expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1588">Espressione regolare con caratteri di escape</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1588">Escaped Regular Expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1589">Le espressioni regolari usate nel routing spesso iniziano con l'accento circonflesso (`^`) e corrispondono alla posizione iniziale della stringa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1589">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the caret (`^`) character and match starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1590">Le espressioni spesso terminano con il segno di dollaro (`$`) e corrispondono alla fine della stringa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1590">The expressions often end with the dollar sign (`$`) character and match end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1591">I caratteri `^` e `$` consentono di verificare che l'espressione regolare corrisponda all'intero valore del parametro di route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1591">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression match the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1592">Senza i caratteri `^` e `$` l'espressione regolare corrisponde a qualsiasi sottostringa all'interno della stringa e spesso questo non è il risultato desiderato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1592">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression match any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1593">La tabella seguente include alcuni esempi e descrive perché si verifica o non si verifica la corrispondenza.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1593">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1594">Expression</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1594">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1595">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1595">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1596">Corrispondente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1596">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1597">Commento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1597">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1598">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1598">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1599">Sì</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1599">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1600">Corrispondenze di sottostringhe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1600">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1601">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1601">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1602">Sì</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1602">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1603">Corrispondenze di sottostringhe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1603">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1604">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1604">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1605">Sì</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1605">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1606">Corrisponde all'espressione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1606">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1607">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1607">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1608">Sì</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1608">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1609">Senza distinzione maiuscole/minuscole</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1609">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1610">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1610">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1611">No</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1611">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1612">Vedere `^` e `$` sopra</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1612">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1613">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1613">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1614">No</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1614">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1615">Vedere `^` e `$` sopra</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1615">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1616">Per altre informazioni sulla sintassi delle espressioni regolari, vedere [Espressioni regolari di .NET Framework](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1616">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1617">Per limitare un parametro a un set noto di valori possibili, usare un'espressione regolare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1617">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1618">Ad esempio, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` verifica la corrispondenza del valore di route `action` solo con `list`, `get` o `create`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1618">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1619">Se viene passata nel dizionario di vincoli, la stringa `^(list|get|create)$` è equivalente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1619">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1620">Anche i vincoli passati nel dizionario di vincoli (non inline all'interno di un modello) che non corrispondono a uno dei vincoli noti vengono considerati espressioni regolari.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1620">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary (not inline within a template) that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

## <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-1621">Vincoli di route personalizzati</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1621">Custom Route Constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1622">Oltre ai vincoli di route predefiniti, è possibile creare vincoli di route personalizzati implementando l'interfaccia <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1622">In addition to the built-in route constraints, custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1623">L'interfaccia <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> contiene un singolo metodo, `Match`, che restituisce `true` se il vincolo viene soddisfatto e `false` in caso contrario.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1623">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface contains a single method, `Match`, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1624">Per usare un'interfaccia <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> personalizzata, il tipo di vincolo di route deve essere registrato con la proprietà <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> dell'app nel contenitore di servizi dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1624">To use a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the app's service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1625"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> è un dizionario che esegue il mapping delle chiavi dei vincoli di route alle implementazioni di <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> che convalidano tali vincoli.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1625">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1626">La proprietà <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> di un'app può essere aggiornata in `Startup.ConfigureServices` come parte di una chiamata [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) o configurando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> direttamente con `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1626">An app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1627">Ad esempio,</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1627">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    options.ConstraintMap.Add("customName", typeof(MyCustomConstraint));
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1628">Il vincolo può quindi essere applicato alle route nel modo consueto, usando il nome specificato al momento della registrazione del tipo di vincolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1628">The constraint can then be applied to routes in the usual manner, using the name specified when registering the constraint type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1629">Ad esempio,</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1629">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
[HttpGet("{id:customName}")]
public ActionResult<string> Get(string id)
```

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-1630">Riferimento per la generazione di URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1630">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1631">L'esempio seguente mostra come generare un collegamento a una route usando un dizionario di valori di route e un elemento <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1631">The following example shows how to generate a link to a route given a dictionary of route values and a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_Dictionary)]

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1632">L'elemento <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generato alla fine dell'esempio precedente è `/package/create/123`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1632">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generated at the end of the preceding sample is `/package/create/123`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1633">Il dizionario fornisce i valori di route `operation` e `id` del modello "Track Package Route", `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1633">The dictionary supplies the `operation` and `id` route values of the "Track Package Route" template, `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1634">Per informazioni dettagliate, vedere il codice di esempio nella sezione [Usare il middleware di routing](#use-routing-middleware) oppure l'[app di esempio](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1634">For details, see the sample code in the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section or the [sample app](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1635">Il secondo parametro per il costruttore <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> è una raccolta di *valori di ambiente*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1635">The second parameter to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> constructor is a collection of *ambient values*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1636">I valori di ambiente sono utili poiché limitano il numero di valori che uno sviluppatore deve specificare all'interno del contesto di una richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1636">Ambient values are convenient to use because they limit the number of values a developer must specify within a request context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1637">I valori di route correnti della richiesta corrente sono considerati valori di ambiente per la generazione del collegamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1637">The current route values of the current request are considered ambient values for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1638">Nell'azione `About` di un'app ASP.NET Core MVC di `HomeController`, non è necessario specificare il valore di route del controller per collegarsi all'azione `Index`. Viene usato il valore di ambiente &mdash;.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1638">In an ASP.NET Core MVC app's `About` action of the `HomeController`, you don't need to specify the controller route value to link to the `Index` action&mdash;the ambient value of `Home` is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1639">I valori di ambiente che non corrispondono a un parametro vengono ignorati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1639">Ambient values that don't match a parameter are ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1640">I valori di ambiente vengono ignorati anche quando un valore specificato in modo esplicito esegue l'override del valore di ambiente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1640">Ambient values are also ignored when an explicitly provided value overrides the ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1641">La corrispondenza si verifica da sinistra a destra nell'URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1641">Matching occurs from left to right in the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1642">I valori specificati in modo esplicito ma che non corrispondono a un segmento della route vengono aggiunti alla stringa di query.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1642">Values explicitly provided but that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1643">La tabella seguente illustra il risultato ottenuto quando si usa il modello di route `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1643">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1644">Valori di ambiente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1644">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1645">Valori espliciti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1645">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1646">Risultato</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1646">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1647">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1647">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1648">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1648">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1649">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1649">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1650">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1650">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |
| <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1651">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1651">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1652">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1652">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1653">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1653">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1654">action = "About", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1654">action = "About", color = "Red"</span></span>        | `/Home/About?color=Red` |

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1655">Se una route ha un valore predefinito che non corrisponde a un parametro e tale valore viene specificato in modo esplicito, deve corrispondere al valore predefinito:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1655">If a route has a default value that doesn't correspond to a parameter and that value is explicitly provided, it must match the default value:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute("blog_route", "blog/{*slug}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadPost" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1656">La generazione dei collegamenti genera un collegamento per questa route quando vengono specificati i valori corrispondenti per `controller` e `action`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1656">Link generation only generates a link for this route when the matching values for `controller` and `action` are provided.</span></span>

## <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="3658d-1657">Segmenti complessi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1657">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3658d-1658">I segmenti complessi (ad esempio, `[Route("/x{token}y")]`), vengono elaborati individuando corrispondenze per i valori letterali da destra a sinistra in modalità non-greedy.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1658">Complex segments (for example `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) are processed by matching up literals from right to left in a non-greedy way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1659">Vedere [questo codice](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) per una spiegazione dettagliata di come vengono confrontati i segmenti complessi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1659">See [this code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) for a detailed explanation of how complex segments are matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3658d-1660">L'[esempio di codice](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) non viene usato da ASP.NET Core, ma offre una spiegazione esauriente dei segmenti complessi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3658d-1660">The [code sample](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) is not used by ASP.NET Core, but it provides a good explanation of complex segments.</span></span>


::: moniker-end
